add_namespace = Ntribes
#add_namespace = Ntribes_news

country_event = { # Centralization Process (beginning)
	id = Ntribes.1
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.1"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = 0.025
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = 0.025
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_political_power = 75
			}
			
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = NTR_steps_towards_centralization_idea
				add_idea = NTR_uncompleted_centralization_idea
			}
			
			add_ideas = NTR_society_increase_upkeep_hidden_idea
			
			country_event = {
				id = Ntribes.2
				days = 60
				random = 240
			}
			
			country_event = {
				id = Ntribes.991
				days = 30
				random = 120
			}
			
			country_event = Ntribes.588
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.1.t
	desc = Ntribes.1.d
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { # The North is Changing
		name = Ntribes.1.a
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = 0.025
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = 0.025
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_political_power = 75
			}
			
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = NTR_steps_towards_centralization_idea
				add_idea = NTR_uncompleted_centralization_idea
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Centralization Process (middle)
	id = Ntribes.2
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.2"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = 0.025
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = 0.025
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_political_power = 50
			}
			
			remove_ideas = NTR_uncompleted_centralization_idea # fascism #???
			
			country_event = {
				id = Ntribes.3
				days = 120
				random = 480
			}
			
			country_event = Ntribes.588
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.2.t
	
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = communism }
		}
		
		text = Ntribes.2.d_a
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_government = communism
		}
		
		text = Ntribes.2.d_b
	}
	
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		check_variable = { EaW_society_development_var < 3 }
		
		NOT = { has_government = neutrality }
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { # Change is sometimes painful
		name = Ntribes.2.a
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = 0.025
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = 0.025
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_political_power = 50
			}
			
			remove_ideas = NTR_uncompleted_centralization_idea
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Centralization Process (end)
	id = Ntribes.3
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.3"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = 0.025
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = 0.025
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_political_power = 50
			}
			
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = communal_society2
				add_idea = agrarian_society
			}
			
			remove_ideas = NTR_society_increase_upkeep_hidden_idea
			
			add_to_variable = { NTR_VED_HLR_guilds_power_var = 1 }
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_poverty = yes
				}
				
				set_country_flag = can_improve_poverty
			}
			
			country_event = Ntribes.588
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.3.t
	
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_government = democratic
		}
		
		text = Ntribes.3.d_a
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_government = communism
		}
		
		text = Ntribes.3.d_b
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_government = fascism
		}
		
		text = Ntribes.3.d_c
	}
	
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		check_variable = { EaW_society_development_var < 3 }
		
		NOT = { has_government = neutrality }
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { # Though I work the fields, at least I eat well
		name = Ntribes.3.a
		
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = fascism }
		}
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = 0.025
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = 0.025
				}
			}
			
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = communal_society2
				add_idea = agrarian_society
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_poverty = yes
				}
				
				unlock_decision_tooltip = improve_poverty_decision
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = Ntribes.3.b
		
		trigger = {
			has_government = fascism
		}
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_political_power = 50
			
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = communal_society2
				add_idea = agrarian_society
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_poverty = yes
				}
				
				unlock_decision_tooltip = improve_poverty_decision
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Choose investor (VED, FAW or others)
	id = Ntribes.4
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.4" }
	title = Ntribes.4.t
	desc = Ntribes.4.d
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { # VED
		name = Ntribes.4.a
		
		trigger = {
			VED = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject = no
				has_government = democratic
				
				is_not_a_potential_enemy_and_has_not_war_with_ROOT = yes
			}
		}
		
		add_political_power = -50
		
		add_ideas = NTR_VED_science_base_investments_idea
		
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { # 80-100
				id = Ntribes.7
				days = 80
				random = 480
			}
			
			VED = { country_event = Ntribes.50 }
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = NTR_AI_TRADE
					
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NTR_ai_behavior
						option = TRADE
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # FAW
		name = Ntribes.4.b
		
		trigger = {
			FAW = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject = no
				has_government = democratic
				
				is_not_a_potential_enemy_and_has_not_war_with_ROOT = yes
				
				NOT = { country_exists = FAT }
			}
		}
		
		add_political_power = -50
		
		add_ideas = NTR_FAW_science_base_investments_idea
		
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { # 80-100
				id = Ntribes.7
				days = 80
				random = 480
			}
			
			FAW = { country_event = Ntribes.50 }
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				
				VED = {
					OR = {
						exists = no
						is_subject = yes
						NOT = { has_government = democratic }
						
						is_a_potential_enemy_or_has_war_with_ROOT = yes
					}
				}
				
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = NTR_AI_VEDINA
					
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NTR_ai_behavior
						option = VEDINA
					}
					
					AND = {
						is_historical_focus_on = yes
						
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = NTR_ai_behavior
							option = DEFAULT
						}
					}
				}
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = NTR_AI_TRADE
					
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NTR_ai_behavior
						option = TRADE
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Others
		name = Ntribes.4.c
		
		add_political_power = -75
		
		add_ideas = NTR_science_base_investments_democratic_idea
		
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { # 120-150
				id = Ntribes.7
				days = 120
				random = 720
			}
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				
				OR = {
					VED = {
						exists = yes
						is_subject = no
						has_government = democratic
						
						is_not_a_potential_enemy_and_has_not_war_with_ROOT = yes
					}
					
					FAW = {
						exists = yes
						is_subject = no
						has_government = democratic
						
						is_not_a_potential_enemy_and_has_not_war_with_ROOT = yes
						
						NOT = { country_exists = FAT }
					}
				}
				
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = NTR_AI_VEDINA
					
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NTR_ai_behavior
						option = VEDINA
					}
					
					AND = {
						is_historical_focus_on = yes
						
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = NTR_ai_behavior
							option = DEFAULT
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # The First Scientists
	id = Ntribes.7
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.7"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = poor_science_base
				add_idea = better_science_base
			}
			
			set_country_flag = better_science_base_unlocked
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = NTR_science_base_investments_democratic_idea
					}
					
					remove_ideas = NTR_science_base_investments_democratic_idea
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = NTR_VED_science_base_investments_idea
					}
					
					remove_ideas = NTR_VED_science_base_investments_idea
					
					VED = { country_event = Ntribes.52 }
				}
				else = {
					remove_ideas = NTR_FAW_science_base_investments_idea
					
					FAW = { country_event = Ntribes.52 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = NTR_SRS_science_base_investments_idea
				}
				
				remove_ideas = NTR_SRS_science_base_investments_idea
				
				SRS = { country_event = Ntribes.52 }
			}
			else = {
				remove_ideas = NTR_science_base_investments_communism_idea
			}
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.7.t
	desc = Ntribes.7.d
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_government = democratic
			has_government = communism
		}
		
		has_idea = poor_science_base
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = Ntribes.7.a
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = poor_science_base
				add_idea = better_science_base
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = NTR_science_base_investments_democratic_idea
					}
					
					remove_ideas = NTR_science_base_investments_democratic_idea
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = NTR_VED_science_base_investments_idea
					}
					
					remove_ideas = NTR_VED_science_base_investments_idea
					
					add_opinion_modifier = {
						target = VED
						modifier = NTR_helped_in_the_development
					}
				}
				else = {
					remove_ideas = NTR_FAW_science_base_investments_idea
					
					add_opinion_modifier = {
						target = FAW
						modifier = NTR_helped_in_the_development
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = NTR_SRS_science_base_investments_idea
				}
				
				remove_ideas = NTR_SRS_science_base_investments_idea
				
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = SRS
					modifier = NTR_helped_in_the_development
				}
			}
			else = {
				remove_ideas = NTR_science_base_investments_communism_idea
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Literacy for All
	id = Ntribes.8
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.8" }
	title = Ntribes.8.t
	desc = Ntribes.8.d
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { # There is still a place for the elders
		name = Ntribes.8.a
		
		add_political_power = -75
		
		custom_effect_tooltip = delayed_decrease_illiteracy_tt
		
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { # 60-70
				id = Ntribes.9
				days = 60
				random = 240
			}
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				
				has_government = communism
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # We must go all the way
		name = Ntribes.8.b
		
		add_stability = -0.025
		add_political_power = -125
		
		custom_effect_tooltip = delayed_decrease_illiteracy_tt
		
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { # 80-95
				id = Ntribes.9
				days = 80
				random = 360
			}
			
			set_country_flag = NTR_new_education_doctrine
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				
				has_government = democratic
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Making Progress
	id = Ntribes.9
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.9"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = 0.05
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = 0.05
				}
			}
			
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = lack_of_scientists
				add_idea = lack_of_scientists1
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NTR_new_education_doctrine
				}
				
				country_event = { # 80-95
					id = Ntribes.10
					days = 80
					random = 360
				}
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { # 60-70
					id = Ntribes.10
					days = 60
					random = 240
				}
			}
			
			country_event = Ntribes.588
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.9.t
	desc = Ntribes.9.d
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_idea = lack_of_scientists
		
		OR = {
			has_government = democratic
			has_government = communism
		}
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = Ntribes.9.a
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = 0.05
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = 0.05
				}
			}
			
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = lack_of_scientists
				add_idea = lack_of_scientists1
			}
			
			custom_effect_tooltip = delayed_decrease_illiteracy_tt
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # A Literate North
	id = Ntribes.10
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.10"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = 0.05
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = 0.05
				}
			}
			
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = lack_of_scientists1
				add_idea = lack_of_scientists2
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NTR_new_education_doctrine
				}
				
				add_tech_bonus = {
					name = electronics_bonus
					bonus = 0.2
					category = electronics
				}
				add_tech_bonus = {
					name = industrial_bonus
					bonus = 0.2
					uses = 3
					category = industry
				}
			}
			
			country_event = Ntribes.588
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.10.t
	desc = Ntribes.10.d
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_idea = lack_of_scientists1
		
		OR = {
			has_government = democratic
			has_government = communism
		}
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = Ntribes.10.a
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = 0.05
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = 0.05
				}
			}
			
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = lack_of_scientists1
				add_idea = lack_of_scientists2
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NTR_new_education_doctrine
				}
				
				add_tech_bonus = {
					name = electronics_bonus
					bonus = 0.2
					category = electronics
				}
				add_tech_bonus = {
					name = industrial_bonus
					bonus = 0.2
					uses = 3
					category = industry
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

					has_country_flag = NTR_AI_TRADE

						rule = NTR_ai_behavior
						option = TRADE

		}
	}
	
	option = { # "Open our Doors to All"
		name = Ntribes.11.b
		
		add_political_power = -50
		
		custom_effect_tooltip = NTR_search_for_investors_tooltip
		
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = Ntribes.98
				days = 3
				random = 24
			}
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				
				VED = {
					exists = yes
					is_subject = no
					has_government = democratic
				}
				
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = NTR_AI_VEDINA
					
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NTR_ai_behavior
						option = VEDINA
					}
					
					AND = {
						is_historical_focus_on = yes
						
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = NTR_ai_behavior
							option = DEFAULT
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	immediate = {

					FROM = { tag = ROOT }
				}
				
				add_political_power = -50
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = 0.025
				}
			}
			else = {
				NTR_up_to_pre_industrial_FROM_effect = yes
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = 0.02
				}
				
				FROM = { country_event = Ntribes.56 }
			}
			
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = agrarian_society6
				add_idea = pre_industrial_society
			}
			
			add_to_variable = { NTR_VED_HLR_guilds_power_var = 1 }
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_poverty = yes
				}
				
				set_country_flag = can_improve_poverty
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NTR_up_to_pre_industrial_not_completed
				}
				
				clr_country_flag = NTR_up_to_pre_industrial_not_completed
			}
			
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NTR_up_to_pre_industrial_helper
				}
				
				clr_country_flag = NTR_up_to_pre_industrial_helper
			}
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.16.t
	desc = Ntribes.16.d
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = Ntribes.16.a
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { tag = ROOT }
				}
				
				add_political_power = -50

					ideology = democratic
					popularity = 0.025
				}
			}
			else = {
				NTR_up_to_pre_industrial_FROM_effect = yes
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = 0.02
				}
			}
			
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = agrarian_society6
				add_idea = pre_industrial_society
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_poverty = yes

		}

country_event = { # Request for help
	id = Ntribes.53
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.53" }
	title = Ntribes.53.t
	desc = Ntribes.53.d
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { # Accept
		name = Ntribes.53.a
		
		add_political_power = 50
		
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = 0.025
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = {
				set_country_flag = NTR_VED_up_to_pre_industrial_helper
				
				country_event = Ntribes.12
			}
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 75
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Reject
		name = Ntribes.53.b
		
		trigger = {
			FROM = { NOT = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
		}
		
		add_political_power = -25
		add_stability = -0.025
		
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = { country_event = Ntribes.13 }
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						is_ai = no
						
						has_country_flag = NTR_AI_VEDINA
						
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = NTR_ai_behavior
							option = VEDINA
						}
						
						AND = {
							is_historical_focus_on = yes
							
							has_game_rule = {
								rule = NTR_ai_behavior
								option = DEFAULT
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

				}
				15 = {
					NTR_save_random_state_as_target_for_complex = yes
					
					set_country_flag = {
						flag = NTR_received_construction
						value = 0
					}
				}
				15 = {
					NTR_save_random_state_as_target_for_dockyard = yes
					
					set_country_flag = {
						flag = NTR_received_construction
						value = 1
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.54.t
	desc = Ntribes.54.d
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = Ntribes.54.a
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = NTR_received_construction }
			}
			
			effect_tooltip = {
				add_political_power = 50
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = NTR_received_construction
						value = 0
					}
				}
				
				effect_tooltip = {
					var:NTR_state_with_one_bonus_complex = {
						add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
						
						add_building_construction = {
							type = industrial_complex
							level = 1
							instant_build = yes
						}
					}
				}
				
				hidden_effect = {
					clear_variable = NTR_state_with_one_bonus_complex
				}
			}
			else = {
				effect_tooltip = {
					var:NTR_state_with_one_bonus_dockyard = {
						add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
						
						add_building_construction = {
							type = dockyard
							level = 1
							instant_build = yes
						}
					}
				}
				
				hidden_effect = {
					clear_variable = NTR_state_with_one_bonus_dockyard
				}
			}
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = NTR_received_construction
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Call from the North
	id = Ntribes.55
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.55" }
	title = Ntribes.55.t
	desc = Ntribes.55.d
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = { # Of course we will help them!
		name = Ntribes.55.a
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = modern_society
			}
			
			FROM = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = agrarian_society6
					}
					
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_government = communism
						}
						
						country_event = { # ~60
							id = Ntribes.18
							days = 55
							random = 240
						}
					}
					else = {
						country_event = { # ~60
							id = Ntribes.16
							days = 55
							random = 240
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					country_event = { # ~60
						id = Ntribes.15
						days = 55
						random = 240
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					id = EaW_society_development_var
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
					value = 5
				}
			}
			
			FROM = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = agrarian_society6
					}
					
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_government = communism
						}
						
						country_event = { # ~75
							id = Ntribes.18
							days = 70
							random = 240
						}
					}
					else = {
						country_event = { # ~75
							id = Ntribes.16
							days = 70
							random = 240
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					country_event = { # ~75
						id = Ntribes.15
						days = 70
						random = 240
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			FROM = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = agrarian_society6
					}
					
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_government = communism
						}
						
						country_event = { # ~90
							id = Ntribes.18
							days = 85
							random = 240
						}
					}
					else = {
						country_event = { # ~90
							id = Ntribes.16
							days = 85
							random = 240
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					country_event = { # ~90
						id = Ntribes.15
						days = 85
						random = 240
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NTR_up_to_pre_industrial_helper
			
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NTR_potential_helper
				}
				
				clr_country_flag = NTR_potential_helper
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # *Autistic speech*
		name = Ntribes.55.b
		
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
			
			FROM = { NOT = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NTR_up_to_pre_industrial_autists
			
			FROM = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_government = democratic
					}
					
					country_event = Ntribes.98
				}
				else = {
					country_event = Ntribes.96
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # The investments has paid off ("Trade with All")
	id = Ntribes.56
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.56"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = modern_society
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						any_of_scopes = {
							array = owned_states
							
							is_coastal = yes
							is_controlled_by = ROOT
						}
					}
					
					random_list = {
						80 = {
							set_variable = { political_power_received = 80 }
							
							add_political_power = var:political_power_received
						}
						10 = {
							NTR_save_random_state_as_target_for_complex = yes
							
							set_country_flag = {
								flag = NTR_received_construction
								value = 0
							}
						}
						10 = {

							set_country_flag = {
								flag = NTR_received_construction
								value = 1
							}
						}
					}
				}

						85 = {
							set_variable = { political_power_received = 65 }

country_event = { # Up to Outdated Society (gradations checks)
	id = Ntribes.95
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.95" }
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		check_variable = { EaW_society_development_var > 5 }
		check_variable = { EaW_society_development_var < 6 }
	}
	
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_idea = pre_industrial_society3 }
			}
			
			increase_society_development_gradual = yes
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_government = neutrality
						has_government = fascism
					}
				}
				
				country_event = { # for neu
					id = Ntribes.95
					days = 90
					random = 360
				}
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { # for dem and com
					id = Ntribes.95
					days = 70
					random = 280
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # for all
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_government = fascism }
			}
			
			country_event = Ntribes.22
		}
		else = {
			country_event = Ntribes.411
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #	Calculation for 'Help from Comrades'
	id = Ntribes.96
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.96" }
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_other_country = {
					has_country_flag = NTR_potential_helper
					
					NOT = { has_country_flag = NTR_up_to_pre_industrial_autists }
				}
			}
			
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NTR_potential_helper
					
					NOT = { has_country_flag = NTR_up_to_pre_industrial_autists }
				}
				
				country_event = Ntribes.55
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				any_other_country = {
					has_government = communism
					has_war = no
					exists = yes
					
					check_variable = {
						var = EaW_society_development_var
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
						value = 4
					}
					
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = NTR_up_to_pre_industrial_autists
						
						has_or_is_justifying_wargoal_against_ROOT = yes
						
						ROOT = {
							OR = {
								has_wargoal_against = PREV
								is_justifying_wargoal_against = PREV
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					exists = yes
					has_war = no
					has_government = communism
					
					check_variable = {
						var = EaW_society_development_var
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
						value = 4
					}
					
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = NTR_up_to_pre_industrial_autists
						
						has_or_is_justifying_wargoal_against_ROOT = yes
						
						ROOT = {
							OR = {
								has_wargoal_against = PREV
								is_justifying_wargoal_against = PREV
							}
						}
					}
				}
				
				set_country_flag = NTR_potential_helper
			}
			
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NTR_potential_helper
				}
				
				country_event = Ntribes.55
			}
		}
		else = {
			country_event = {
				id = Ntribes.15
				days = 120
				random = 480
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #	Calculation for 'Trade with SRS'
	id = Ntribes.97
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.97" }
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_government = democratic
			has_government = communism
		}
		
		OR = {
			has_idea = agrarian_society2
			has_idea = agrarian_society3
			has_idea = agrarian_society4
			has_idea = agrarian_society5
			has_idea = agrarian_society6
		}
	}
	
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = communism
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_war = no
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						SRS = {
							exists = yes
							is_subject = no
							has_government = communism
							
							has_war = no
							has_civil_war = no
							
							NOT = {
								has_or_is_justifying_wargoal_against_ROOT = yes
								
								ROOT = {
									OR = {
										has_wargoal_against = PREV
										is_justifying_wargoal_against = PREV
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_idea = agrarian_society6
						}
						
						country_event = Ntribes.18
					}
					else = {
						country_event = Ntribes.17
					}
					
					SRS = { country_event = Ntribes.57 }
				}
			}
			else = { # wait
				set_country_flag = NTR_up_to_pre_industrial_not_completed
			}
		}
		else = {
			country_event = Ntribes.98
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #	Calculation for 'Trade with VED'
	id = Ntribes.99
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.99" }
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_government = democratic
			has_government = communism
		}
		
		OR = {
			has_idea = agrarian_society2
			has_idea = agrarian_society3
			has_idea = agrarian_society4
			has_idea = agrarian_society5
			has_idea = agrarian_society6
		}
	}
	
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = democratic
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_war = no
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						VED = {
							exists = yes
							has_war = no
							is_subject = no
							has_government = democratic
							
							NOT = {
								has_or_is_justifying_wargoal_against_ROOT = yes
								
								ROOT = {
									OR = {
										has_wargoal_against = PREV
										is_justifying_wargoal_against = PREV
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_idea = agrarian_society6
						}
						
						country_event = Ntribes.14
					}
					else = {
						country_event = Ntribes.16
					}
					
					VED = { country_event = Ntribes.54 }
				}
				else = { # to "Trade with All"
					country_event = Ntribes.98
				}
			}
			else = { # wait
				set_country_flag = NTR_up_to_pre_industrial_not_completed
			}
		}
		else = {
			country_event = Ntribes.97
		}
	}
}

##### Harmony events #####
### Internal Events ###

country_event = { # A New Constitution
	id = Ntribes.100
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.100" }
	title = Ntribes.100.t
	desc = Ntribes.100.d
	#picture = 
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { # The last say in all decisions will rest with me
		name = Ntribes.100.a
		
		add_political_power = -100
		add_stability = 0.075
		
		add_ideas = NTR_an_executive_monarchy_idea
		
		set_cosmetic_tag = NTR_monarchy
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				
				VED = {
					OR = {
						exists = no
						is_subject = yes
						
						NOT = {
							has_government = democratic
						}
					}
				}
				
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = NTR_AI_TRADE
					
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NTR_ai_behavior
						option = TRADE
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # The last say rests with the representatives of the tribes
		name = Ntribes.100.b
		
		add_political_power = 150
		add_stability = -0.05
		
		add_ideas = NTR_a_constitutional_monarchy_idea
		
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = democratic
			long_name = NTR_liberal_party_long
			name = NTR_liberal_party
		}
		
		set_cosmetic_tag = NTR_trade
		
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_leader_ideology = liberalism
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				
				VED = {
					exists = yes
					is_subject = no
					has_government = democratic
				}
				
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = NTR_AI_VEDINA
					
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NTR_ai_behavior
						option = VEDINA
					}
					
					AND = {
						is_historical_focus_on = yes
						
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = NTR_ai_behavior
							option = DEFAULT
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Vedina Agrees!
	id = Ntribes.101
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.101" }
	title = Ntribes.101.t
	
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = NTR_reclaim_the_west }
		}
		
		text = Ntribes.101.d_a
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = NTR_reclaim_the_west
		}
		
		text = Ntribes.101.d_b
	}
	
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		name = Ntribes.101.a
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = NTR_reclaim_the_west }
				}
				
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = FROM
					relation = guarantee
					active = yes
				}
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = FROM
					relation = non_aggression_pact
					active = yes
				}
				FROM = {
					diplomatic_relation = {
						country = ROOT
						relation = guarantee
						active = yes
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = FROM
					relation = non_aggression_pact
					active = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Research agreement
	id = Ntribes.105
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.105"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = NTR_VED_maintaining_relations_low_hidden_idea
				}
				
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = NTR_VED_maintaining_relations_low_hidden_idea
					add_idea = NTR_VED_maintaining_relations_medium_hidden_idea
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = NTR_VED_maintaining_relations_low_hidden_idea
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_idea = NTR_VED_democratic_check_hidden_idea }
					}
					
					add_ideas = NTR_VED_democratic_check_hidden_idea
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.105.t
	
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			FROM = { is_in_tech_sharing_group = Northern_griffonia_science_organisation_democratic_full }
		}
		
		text = Ntribes.105.d_a
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			FROM = { is_in_tech_sharing_group = Northern_griffonia_science_organisation_democratic }
		}
		
		text = Ntribes.105.d_b
	}
	
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { # A pleasant surprise
		name = Ntribes.105.a
		
		trigger = {
			FROM = { is_in_tech_sharing_group = Northern_griffonia_science_organisation_democratic_full }
		}
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_political_power = 50
			
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = 0.025
			}
			
			add_to_tech_sharing_group = Northern_griffonia_science_organisation_democratic_full
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Well, it is better than nothing
		name = Ntribes.105.b
		
		trigger = {
			FROM = { is_in_tech_sharing_group = Northern_griffonia_science_organisation_democratic }
		}
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_political_power = -25
			
			add_to_tech_sharing_group = Northern_griffonia_science_organisation_democratic
		}
	}
}

	id = Ntribes.106
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.106"

			if = {
				limit = {

				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = NTR_VED_maintaining_relations_medium_hidden_idea
					add_idea = NTR_VED_maintaining_relations_high_hidden_idea
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = NTR_VED_maintaining_relations_low_hidden_idea
				}
				
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = NTR_VED_maintaining_relations_low_hidden_idea
					add_idea = NTR_VED_maintaining_relations_medium_hidden_idea
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = NTR_VED_maintaining_relations_low_hidden_idea
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_idea = NTR_VED_democratic_check_hidden_idea }
					}
					
					add_ideas = NTR_VED_democratic_check_hidden_idea
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.106.t
	
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			FROM = { has_idea = VED_NTR_joint_development_idea_full_idea }
		}
		
		text = Ntribes.106.d_a
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			FROM = { has_idea = VED_NTR_joint_development_idea }
		}
		
		text = Ntribes.106.d_b
	}
	
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { # Now everything will change
		name = Ntribes.106.a
		
		trigger = {
			FROM = { has_idea = VED_NTR_joint_development_idea_full_idea }
		}
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_political_power = 50
			
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = 0.025
			}
			
			add_ideas = NTR_VED_joint_development_idea_full_idea
		}
	}
	option = { # Well, we really asked a lot
		name = Ntribes.106.b
		
		trigger = {
			FROM = { has_idea = VED_NTR_joint_development_idea }
		}
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_political_power = -25
			
			add_ideas = NTR_VED_joint_development_idea
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Together in the Future
	id = Ntribes.107
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.107"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = NTR_insignificant_isolationism_idea
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					VED = { NOT = { has_idea = VED_NTR_maintaining_relations_high_hidden_idea } }
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						VED = { has_idea = VED_NTR_maintaining_relations_medium_hidden_idea }
					}
					
					add_timed_idea = {
						idea = NTR_insignificant_isolationism_idea
						days = 60
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						VED = { has_idea = VED_NTR_maintaining_relations_low_hidden_idea }
					}
					
					add_timed_idea = {
						idea = NTR_insignificant_isolationism_idea
						days = 180
					}
				}
				else = {
					add_timed_idea = {
						idea = NTR_insignificant_isolationism_idea
						days = 360
					}
				}
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_idea = NTR_VED_democratic_check_hidden_idea }
				}
				
				add_ideas = NTR_VED_democratic_check_hidden_idea
			}
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.107.t
	desc = Ntribes.107.d
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = Ntribes.107.a
		
		trigger = {
			VED = { has_idea = VED_NTR_maintaining_relations_high_hidden_idea }
		}
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			remove_ideas = NTR_insignificant_isolationism_idea
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = Ntribes.107.b
		
		trigger = {
			VED = { has_idea = VED_NTR_maintaining_relations_medium_hidden_idea }
		}
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = NTR_insignificant_isolationism_idea
				days = 60
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = Ntribes.107.c
		
		trigger = {
			VED = { has_idea = VED_NTR_maintaining_relations_low_hidden_idea }
		}
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = NTR_insignificant_isolationism_idea
				days = 180
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = Ntribes.107.e
		
		trigger = {
			VED = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_idea = VED_NTR_maintaining_relations_low_hidden_idea
						has_idea = VED_NTR_maintaining_relations_medium_hidden_idea
						has_idea = VED_NTR_maintaining_relations_high_hidden_idea
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = NTR_insignificant_isolationism_idea
				days = 360
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # The Best Possible News
	id = Ntribes.108
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.108"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NTR_owns_SRS_cores_flag
			set_country_flag = NTR_SRS_peaceful_integration
			
			add_ideas = NTR_SRS_reclaiming_the_west_beginning_idea
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					542 = { is_demilitarized_zone = yes }
				}
				
				542 = { set_demilitarized_zone = no }
			}
			
			country_event = {
				id = Ntribes.197
				days = 60
				random = 240
			}
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.108.t
	desc = Ntribes.108.d
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = Ntribes.108.a
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			FROM = { transfer_navy = { target = ROOT } }
			
			annex_country = {
				target = FROM
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
			
			add_ideas = NTR_SRS_reclaiming_the_west_beginning_idea
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Submission of the Reds
	id = Ntribes.110
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.110"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = NTR_SRS_reclaiming_the_west_beginning_idea
				add_idea = NTR_SRS_reclaiming_the_west_middle_idea
			}
			
			save_current_manpower = yes
			
			set_variable = { divider = -50 }
			set_variable = { randomizer = 0.2 }
			set_variable = { rounder = 100 }

				set_variable = { population_var = state_population }
				population_calculator_multifunctional = yes
				add_manpower = var:population_var
			}

				set_variable = { population_var = state_population }
				population_calculator_multifunctional = yes
				add_manpower = var:population_var
			}

				set_variable = { population_var = state_population }
				population_calculator_multifunctional = yes
				add_manpower = var:population_var
			}

				set_variable = { population_var = state_population }

		}

			effect_tooltip = { add_manpower = var:population_var }

		542 = {
			effect_tooltip = { add_manpower = var:population_var }
			clear_variable = population_var
		}
		601 = {
			effect_tooltip = { add_manpower = var:population_var }
			clear_variable = population_var

		name = Ntribes.152.a
		
		add_political_power = -100

			if = {

				}

					remove_idea = VED_NTR_maintaining_relations_medium_hidden_idea
					add_idea = VED_NTR_maintaining_relations_high_hidden_idea
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = VED_NTR_maintaining_relations_low_hidden_idea
				}
				
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = VED_NTR_maintaining_relations_low_hidden_idea
					add_idea = VED_NTR_maintaining_relations_medium_hidden_idea
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = VED_NTR_maintaining_relations_low_hidden_idea
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_idea = VED_NTR_democratic_check_hidden_idea }
					}
					
					add_ideas = VED_NTR_democratic_check_hidden_idea
				}
			}
		}
		
		FROM = {
			add_ideas = NTR_VED_joint_development_idea_full_idea

				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic

			}

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.171" }
	title = Ntribes.171.t
	
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			FROM = { has_completed_focus = NTR_glory_to_the_north }
		}
		
		text = Ntribes.171.d_a
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			FROM = { has_completed_focus = NTR_the_polar_star }
		}
		
		text = Ntribes.171.d_b
	}
	
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { # Accept
		name = Ntribes.171.a
		
		trigger = {
			FROM = { has_completed_focus = NTR_glory_to_the_north }
		}
		
		add_political_power = -25
		
		diplomatic_relation = {
			country = FROM
			relation = non_aggression_pact
			active = yes
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = { country_event = Ntribes.134 }
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Accept
		name = Ntribes.171.b
		
		trigger = {
			FROM = { has_completed_focus = NTR_the_polar_star }
		}
		
		add_political_power = -50
		
		diplomatic_relation = {
			country = FROM
			relation = non_aggression_pact
			active = yes
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NTR_trade_completed
			
			FROM = { country_event = Ntribes.134 }
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = Ntribes.171.c
		
		FROM = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = refused_to_cooperate
			}
			
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = Ntribes.135
			}
		}
	}
}


country_event = { # Trade agreement
	id = Ntribes.172
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.172" }
	title = Ntribes.172.t
	
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			is_major = yes
		}
		
		text = Ntribes.172.d_a
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			is_major = no
		}
		
		text = Ntribes.172.d_b
	}
	
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = { # Accept
		name = Ntribes.172.a
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_major = yes
			}
			
			add_political_power = -50
		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = -25
		}
		
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = trading
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = trading
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NTR_trade_completed
			
			FROM = { country_event = Ntribes.132 }
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 80
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Reject
		name = Ntribes.172.b
		
		FROM = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = refused_to_cooperate
			}
			
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = Ntribes.133
			}
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				
				has_government = democratic
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # NTR consulate constructed
	id = Ntribes.173
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.173"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tag = event_target:equestria
						tag = event_target:RivFed
					}
				}
				
				set_country_flag = Majors_consulate_constructed
			}
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.173.t
	desc = Ntribes.173.d
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		name = Ntribes.173.a
		
		add_political_power = 50
		add_stability = 0.025
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			CAPITAL_SCOPE = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					static_modifiers = { consulate }
					province = {
						all_provinces = yes
						limit_to_victory_point = yes # todefine for every CAPITAL scope... #???
					}
				}
			}
			
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = FROM
				modifier = RIV_friendship_delegation
			}
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = FROM
				modifier = RIV_friendship_delegation
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Apply for the expansion of NTR diplomatic property
	id = Ntribes.174
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.174" }
	title = Ntribes.174.t
	desc = Ntribes.174.d
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = { # Grant lands
		name = Ntribes.174.a
		
		add_political_power = -50
		
		CAPITAL_SCOPE = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					free_building_slots = {
						building = industrial_complex
						size < 1
						include_locked = no
					}
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						arms_factory > 0
					}
					
					remove_building = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = 1
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						dockyard > 0
					}
					
					remove_building = {
						type = dockyard
						level = 1
					}
				}
				else = {
					remove_building = {
						type = industrial_complex
						level = 1
					}
				}
			}
			
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = -1
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NTR_can_expand_diplomatic_property
			
			FROM = { country_event = Ntribes.136 }
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
	}
	
	option = { # They ask too much
		name = Ntribes.174.b
		
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = { country_event = Ntribes.137 }
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # The Second Coming
	id = Ntribes.177
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.177"
		
		set_variable = { communards_vs_internationalists_support_var = communards_support_var }
		divide_variable = { communards_vs_internationalists_support_var = internationalists_support_var }
		multiply_variable = { communards_vs_internationalists_support_var = communards_vs_internationalists_support_var }
		
		set_variable = { internationalists_vs_communards_support_var = internationalists_support_var }
		divide_variable = { internationalists_vs_communards_support_var = communards_support_var }
		multiply_variable = { internationalists_vs_communards_support_var = internationalists_vs_communards_support_var }
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.177.t
	desc = Ntribes.177.d
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { # We agree
		name = Ntribes.177.a
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
				FROM = { is_ai = yes }
			}
			
			FROM = { change_tag_from = ROOT }
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = GAME_OVER_TT
		}
		
		transfer_navy = { target = FROM }
		
		FROM = {
			annex_country = {
				target = ROOT
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
			
			country_event = Ntribes.148
		}
		
		clear_variable = communards_vs_internationalists_support_var
		clear_variable = internationalists_vs_communards_support_var
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			
			modifier = {
				factor = var:communards_vs_internationalists_support_var
				
				has_variable = communards_vs_internationalists_support_var
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # We will fight to the end!
		name = Ntribes.177.b
		
		FROM = { country_event = Ntribes.147 }
		
		clear_variable = communards_vs_internationalists_support_var
		clear_variable = internationalists_vs_communards_support_var
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			
			modifier = {
				factor = var:internationalists_vs_communards_support_var
				
				has_variable = internationalists_vs_communards_support_var
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				
				NOT = { has_idea = SRS_northern_clashes }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Check to include SRS in NTR during the war with a strong opponent
	id = Ntribes.193
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war = yes
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						surrender_progress > 0.5
						
						AND = {
							enemies_strength_ratio > 1.5
							surrender_progress > 0.25
						}
						AND = {
							enemies_strength_ratio > 2
							surrender_progress > 0.1
						}
					}
					
					NOT = { has_war_with = NTR }
				}
				
				NTR = { country_event = Ntribes.149 }
				
				clr_country_flag = NTR_SRS_reclaiming_the_west_beginning_idea_check_on
				
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: self-triggering event Ntribes.193 stopped"
			}
			else = {
				country_event = {
					id = Ntribes.193
					days = 7
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			clr_country_flag = NTR_SRS_reclaiming_the_west_beginning_idea_check_on
			
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: self-triggering event Ntribes.193 stopped"
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Recalculation of overabundance of offsite dockyards and/or complexes
	id = Ntribes.194
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.194" }
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		add_offsite_building = {
			type = dockyard
			level = 3
		}
		add_offsite_building = {
			type = industrial_complex
			level = -2
		}
		
		subtract_from_variable = { NTR_bonus_complexes = 2 }
		add_to_variable = { NTR_not_equals_dockyards_calculation = 3 }
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { NTR_not_equals_dockyards_calculation < 4 }
					check_variable = { NTR_bonus_complexes < 2 }
				}
			}
			
			country_event = Ntribes.195
		}
		
		else = {
			country_event = Ntribes.194
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Recalculation of lack of offsite dockyards and/or complexes
	id = Ntribes.195
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.195" }
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		clear_variable = NTR_not_equals_dockyards_calculation
		
		multiply_variable = { NTR_received_offsite_dockyards = -1 }
		
		add_offsite_building = {
			type = dockyard
			level = var:NTR_received_offsite_dockyards
		}
		
		set_variable = { NTR_received_offsite_dockyards = NTR_num_dockyards_per_agreements_var }
		
		add_offsite_building = {
			type = dockyard
			level = var:NTR_received_offsite_dockyards
		}
		
		clear_variable = NTR_num_dockyards_per_agreements_var
		
		country_event = {
			id = Ntribes.196
			days = 7
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Check for received bonus dockyards
	id = Ntribes.196
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.196" }
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		set_variable = { NTR_num_dockyards_per_agreements_var = 0 }
		
		every_other_country = { # array?
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = NTR_friends_check_for_bonus_dockyards
				
				exists = yes
				is_subject = no
				has_government = democratic
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_major = yes
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							tag = event_target:equestria
							tag = event_target:RivFed
						}
					}
					
					add_to_variable = { ROOT.NTR_num_dockyards_per_agreements_var = 6 }
				}
				else = {
					add_to_variable = { ROOT.NTR_num_dockyards_per_agreements_var = 3 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_to_variable = { ROOT.NTR_num_dockyards_per_agreements_var = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		divide_variable = { NTR_num_dockyards_per_agreements_var = 3 } # 1 dockyard ~ 3 agreement (because of round)
		round_variable = NTR_num_dockyards_per_agreements_var
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = NTR_received_offsite_dockyards
					compare = not_equals
					value = NTR_num_dockyards_per_agreements_var
				}
			}
			
			set_variable = { NTR_not_equals_dockyards_calculation = NTR_received_offsite_dockyards }
			subtract_from_variable = { NTR_not_equals_dockyards_calculation = NTR_num_dockyards_per_agreements_var }
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { NTR_not_equals_dockyards_calculation > 3 }
					check_variable = { NTR_bonus_complexes > 1 }
				}
				
				country_event = Ntribes.194
			}
			else = {
				country_event = Ntribes.195
			}
		}
		else = {
			clear_variable = NTR_num_dockyards_per_agreements_var
			
			country_event = {
				id = Ntribes.196
				days = 7
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Check for Integration Gradation
	id = Ntribes.197
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.197" }
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_government = communism }
	}
	
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = NTR_owns_SRS_cores_flag
				
				has_war = no
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = NTR_SRS_reclaiming_the_west_end_idea
				}
				
				country_event = Ntribes.112
			}
			else = {
				country_event = Ntribes.111
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = NTR_SRS_reclaiming_the_west_beginning_idea_not_completed
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Check for bonus PP from Vedinian Guild
	id = Ntribes.198
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.198" }
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { NTR_VED_HLR_guilds_power_var = 0 }
			}
			
			NTR = {
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NTR_bonus_PP_from_vedinian_guild }
				
				clear_variable = NTR_bonus_PP_from_VED_guild_var
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { NTR_VED_HLR_guilds_power_var = 1 }
			}
			
			NTR = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NTR_bonus_PP_from_vedinian_guild }
					}
					
					remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NTR_bonus_PP_from_vedinian_guild }
				}
				
				set_variable = { NTR_bonus_PP_from_VED_guild_var = 0.05 }
				
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NTR_bonus_PP_from_vedinian_guild }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { NTR_VED_HLR_guilds_power_var = 2 }
			}
			
			NTR = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NTR_bonus_PP_from_vedinian_guild }
					}
					
					remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NTR_bonus_PP_from_vedinian_guild }
				}
				
				set_variable = { NTR_bonus_PP_from_VED_guild_var = 0.1 }
				
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NTR_bonus_PP_from_vedinian_guild }
			}
		}
		else = {
			NTR = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NTR_bonus_PP_from_vedinian_guild }
					}
					
					remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NTR_bonus_PP_from_vedinian_guild }
				}
				
				set_variable = { NTR_bonus_PP_from_VED_guild_var = 0.15 }
				
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NTR_bonus_PP_from_vedinian_guild }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Question About Our Future
	id = Ntribes.200
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.200" }
	title = Ntribes.200.t
	desc = Ntribes.200.d
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { # We will unite ("United North" branch)
		name = Ntribes.200.a
		
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = NTR_AI_TOWARDS_REVOLUTION
					
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NTR_ai_behavior
						option = TOWARDS_REVOLUTION
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		add_political_power = -50
		
		SRS = {
			country_event = {
				id = Ntribes.250
				hours = 6
				random = 12
			}
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NTR_ai_behavior
						option = DEFAULT
					}
				}
				
				set_country_flag = NTR_SRS_united_north_request
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # We want to maintain self-government ("Towards Revolutions" branch)
		name = Ntribes.200.b
		
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NTR_ai_behavior
						option = UNITED_NORTH
					}
					
					has_country_flag = NTR_AI_UNITED_NORTH
				}
			}
		}
		
		add_political_power = -50
		
		SRS = {
			country_event = {
				id = Ntribes.250

country_event = { # United North
	id = Ntribes.201
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.201"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = {
				every_unit_leader = { set_nationality = ROOT }
				transfer_navy = { target = ROOT }
			}
			
			annex_country = {
				target = FROM
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
			
			set_cosmetic_tag = NTR_SRS_united
			
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Northland General Congress"
				picture = "GeneralCongress.tga"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = democratic_socialism
				traits = { NTR_general_council_trait }
			}

			#	ideology = communism

			#}

			add_ideas = NTR_uneven_development_idea
			
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = NTR_army_of_the_past_millennium_idea
				add_idea = NTR_a_fledgling_modern_army_idea
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = pre_industrial_society
				add_idea = pre_industrial_society2
			}
			
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = FROM
				}
				
				add_core_of = ROOT
			}

				limit = {
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = NTR_establish_a_hierarchy }
				}
				
				add_political_power = -50
				
				complete_national_focus = NTR_establish_a_hierarchy
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = NTR_a_true_army }
				}
				
				add_political_power = -50
				
				complete_national_focus = NTR_a_true_army

					NOT = { has_completed_focus = NTR_revise_combat_tactics }
				}

					NOT = { has_completed_focus = NTR_guns_to_shake_the_earth }

			}

				limit = {
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = NTR_new_rifles }
				}

			}
			if = {

					NOT = { has_completed_focus = NTR_the_panoply_of_war }
				}
				
				unlock_national_focus = NTR_the_panoply_of_war
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = NTR_making_the_most_of_our_potential }
				}
				
				unlock_national_focus = NTR_making_the_most_of_our_potential #check later #???
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = NTR_and_even_more }
				}
				
				add_political_power = -50
				
				complete_national_focus = NTR_and_even_more
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = NTR_a_centralized_northern_army }
				}
				
				add_political_power = -50
				
				complete_national_focus = NTR_a_centralized_northern_army
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = NTR_standardized_weapons }
				}

				complete_national_focus = NTR_standardized_weapons
			}

country_event = { # SRS proposal
	id = Ntribes.250
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.250"
		
		set_variable = { communards_vs_internationalists_support_var = communards_support_var }
		divide_variable = { communards_vs_internationalists_support_var = internationalists_support_var }
		multiply_variable = { communards_vs_internationalists_support_var = communards_vs_internationalists_support_var }
		
		set_variable = { internationalists_vs_communards_support_var = internationalists_support_var }
		divide_variable = { internationalists_vs_communards_support_var = communards_support_var }
		multiply_variable = { internationalists_vs_communards_support_var = internationalists_vs_communards_support_var }
		
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						OR = {
							is_subject_of = ROOT
							
							has_game_rule = {
								rule = NTR_ai_behavior
								option = TOWARDS_REVOLUTION
							}
							
							AND = {
								has_game_rule = {
									rule = NTR_ai_behavior
									option = RANDOM
								}
								
								has_country_flag = NTR_AI_TOWARDS_REVOLUTION
							}
						}
					}
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
					}
					
					diplomatic_relation = {
						country = FROM
						relation = non_aggression_pact
						active = yes
					}
					diplomatic_relation = {
						country = FROM
						relation = guarantee
						active = yes
					}
					ROOT = {
						diplomatic_relation = {
							country = ROOT
							relation = guarantee
							active = yes
						}
					}
				}
				
				country_event = Ntribes.202
			}
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.250.t
	
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			FROM = { has_country_flag = NTR_SRS_united_north_request }
		}
		
		text = Ntribes.250.d_a
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			FROM = { has_country_flag = NTR_SRS_towards_revolution_request }
		}
		
		text = Ntribes.250.d_b
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			FROM = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = NTR_SRS_united_north_request
						has_country_flag = NTR_SRS_towards_revolution_request
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		text = Ntribes.250.d_c
	}
	
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { # We will build a utopia in the northern wastelands together
		name = Ntribes.250.a
		
		trigger = {
			FROM = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = NTR_ai_behavior
							option = TOWARDS_REVOLUTION
						}
						
						AND = {
							has_game_rule = {
								rule = NTR_ai_behavior
								option = RANDOM
							}
							
							has_country_flag = NTR_AI_TOWARDS_REVOLUTION
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
				FROM = { is_ai = yes }
			}
			
			change_tag_from = ROOT
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = GAME_OVER_TT
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			CAPITAL_SCOPE = {
				set_variable = { previous_owner_industry_ratio = 100 }
				
				FROM = {
					ROOT = { paperclip_tech = yes }
				}
			}
		}
		
		FROM = {
			effect_tooltip = {
				annex_country = { target = ROOT }
			}
			
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = Ntribes.201
			}
		}
		
		clear_variable = communards_vs_internationalists_support_var
		clear_variable = internationalists_vs_communards_support_var
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			
			modifier = {
				factor = var:communards_vs_internationalists_support_var
				
				has_variable = communards_vs_internationalists_support_var
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				
				FROM = { has_country_flag = NTR_SRS_towards_revolution_request }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # We will carry the flame of the revolution together
		name = Ntribes.250.b
		
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NTR_ai_behavior
						option = UNITED_NORTH
					}
					
					FROM = {
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = NTR_ai_behavior
							option = RANDOM
						}
						
						has_country_flag = NTR_AI_UNITED_NORTH
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { is_subject = no }
			}
			
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = FROM
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = yes
			}
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = FROM
				relation = guarantee
				active = yes
			}
			FROM = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = ROOT
					relation = guarantee
					active = yes
				}
			}
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = {
				country_event = Ntribes.202
			}
		}
		
		clear_variable = communards_vs_internationalists_support_var
		clear_variable = internationalists_vs_communards_support_var
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			
			modifier = {
				factor = var:internationalists_vs_communards_support_var
				
				has_variable = internationalists_vs_communards_support_var
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				
				FROM = { has_country_flag = NTR_SRS_united_north_request }
			}
		}
	}

				}
				
				add_resource = {
					type = steel
					amount = 14
					state = 480
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.256.t
	desc = Ntribes.256.d

			}
			
			effect_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_government = communism
					}
					
					459 = {
						add_building_construction = {
							type = infrastructure
							level = 2
							instant_build = yes
						}
					}
					475 = {
						add_building_construction = {
							type = infrastructure
							level = 1
							instant_build = yes
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					459 = {
						add_building_construction = {
							type = infrastructure
							level = 2
							instant_build = yes
						}
						
						add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
						
						add_building_construction = {
							type = industrial_complex
							level = 1
							instant_build = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			effect_tooltip = {
				480 = {
					add_building_construction = {
						type = infrastructure
						level = 2
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				474 = {
					add_building_construction = {
						type = infrastructure
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
			}
			
			if = { # Sunstriker shit
				limit = {
					480 = { NOT = { has_state_flag = windford_steel_developed } }
				}
				
				effect_tooltip = {
					add_resource = {
						type = steel
						amount = 14
						state = 480
					}
				}
				
				hidden_effect = {
					480 = { set_state_flag = windford_steel_developed }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	fire_only_once = no

		name = Ntribes.306.a
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_idea = NTR_tensions_between_the_new_and_the_old_idea }
			}
			
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = NTR_resurgent_traditionalism_idea
				add_idea = NTR_tensions_between_the_new_and_the_old_idea
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = -20
			
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = 0.025
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Our Real Destiny
	id = Ntribes.307
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.307"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { # -PP (-750 - -250)
					check_variable = { party_popularity@neutrality > party_popularity@communism }
				}
				
				set_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_multiplier_temp_var = party_popularity@communism }
				divide_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_multiplier_temp_var = party_popularity@neutrality }
				add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_multiplier_temp_var = -1 }
				
				set_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_temp_var = 500 }
			}
			else = { # +PP (-250 - +250)
				set_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_multiplier_temp_var = party_popularity@neutrality }
				divide_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_multiplier_temp_var = party_popularity@communism }
				add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_multiplier_temp_var = -1 }
				
				set_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_temp_var = -500 }
			}
			
			multiply_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_temp_var = NTR_political_power_after_coup_multiplier_temp_var }
			add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_temp_var = -250 }
			add_political_power = NTR_political_power_after_coup_temp_var
			
			retire_country_leader = yes
			
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Remains of the Tribal Council"
				desc = ""
				picture = "Governor.tga" # portrait #???
				expire = "1965.1.1"

				name = "Communal Council"
				desc = ""
				picture = "Governor.tga" # portrait #???
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = marxism
				traits = { NTR_communal_council_trait }
			}
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.307.t
	desc = Ntribes.307.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = Ntribes.307.a
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = communism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Communal Council"
				desc = ""
				picture = "Governor.tga" # portrait #???
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = marxism
				traits = { NTR_communal_council_trait }
			}
		}
	}

country_event = { # Relocation program
	id = Ntribes.448
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.448"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { divider = -15 }
			set_variable = { randomizer = 0.5 }
			
			save_current_manpower = yes
			
			562 = {
				set_variable = { population_k = state_population_k }
				population_calculator_multifunctional_k = yes
				population_calculation_for_sum_k = yes
			}
			574 = {
				set_variable = { population_k = state_population_k }
				population_calculator_multifunctional_k = yes
				population_calculation_for_sum_k = yes
			}
			563	= {
				set_variable = { population_k = state_population_k }
				population_calculator_multifunctional_k = yes
				population_calculation_for_sum_k = yes
			}
			522	= {
				set_variable = { population_k = state_population_k }
				population_calculator_multifunctional_k = yes
				population_calculation_for_sum_k = yes
			}
			
			multiply_variable = { population_sum = -1000 }
			
			set_variable = { divider = 2 }
			set_variable = { randomizer = 0.2 }
			
			set_variable = { population_var = population_sum }
			population_calculator_multifunctional = yes
			
			subtract_from_variable = { population_sum = population_var }
			
			430 = { add_manpower = ROOT.population_var }
			483 = { add_manpower = ROOT.population_sum }
			
			restore_previous_manpower = yes
			
			population_calculator_cleaner_k = yes
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.448.t
	desc = Ntribes.448.d
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = Ntribes.448.a
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			430 = { add_manpower = ROOT.population_var }
			483 = { add_manpower = ROOT.population_sum }
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			clear_variable = population_var
			clear_variable = population_sum
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = Ntribes.499
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.499" }
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Child of the Blizzard"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					has_tech = griffon_race
					
					NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = NTR_enemy_of_griffonkind }
				}
				
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = ROOT
					modifier = NTR_enemy_of_griffonkind
				}
				
				reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = ROOT
					modifier = NTR_enemy_of_griffonkind
				}
				
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = ROOT
					modifier = CHN_Embargo
				}
				
				reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = ROOT
					modifier = CHN_Embargo
				}
			}
			
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_tech = griffon_race }
					
					has_opinion = {
						target = FROM
						value > -20
					}
				}
				
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = ROOT
					modifier = distrustful_relations
				}
				
				reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = ROOT
					modifier = distrustful_relations
				}
			}
			
			country_event = {
				id = Ntribes.499
				days = 14
			}
		}
	}
}

				clear_variable = NTR_traditionalism_influence_offensive_war_stability_factor_var
				
				set_variable = { NTR_traditionalism_influence_political_power_factor_var = -0.5 }
				set_variable = { NTR_traditionalism_influence_stability_factor_var = -0.5 }
				
				set_variable = { NTR_traditionalism_influence_enemy_justify_war_goal_time_var = party_popularity@neutrality }
				
				multiply_variable = { NTR_traditionalism_influence_political_power_factor_var = party_popularity@neutrality }
				multiply_variable = { NTR_traditionalism_influence_stability_factor_var = party_popularity@neutrality }
				
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NTR_traditionalism_influence_dynamic_modifier }
				
				divide_temp_variable = { NTR_united_north_num_bonus_divisions_temp_var = party_popularity@democratic }
				multiply_temp_variable = { NTR_united_north_num_bonus_divisions_temp_var = party_popularity@neutrality }
			}
			else = {
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NTR_harmonic_tribes_dynamic_modifier }
				
				clear_variable = NTR_harmonic_tribes_war_support_factor_var
				clear_variable = NTR_harmonic_tribes_conscription_factor_var
				clear_variable = NTR_harmonic_tribes_offensive_war_stability_factor_var
				
				set_variable = { NTR_harmonic_tribes_political_power_factor_var = -0.5 }
				set_variable = { NTR_harmonic_tribes_stability_factor_var = -0.5 }
				
				multiply_variable = { NTR_harmonic_tribes_political_power_factor_var = party_popularity@democratic }
				multiply_variable = { NTR_harmonic_tribes_stability_factor_var = party_popularity@democratic }
				
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NTR_harmonic_tribes_dynamic_modifier }
				
				divide_temp_variable = { NTR_united_north_num_bonus_divisions_temp_var = party_popularity@neutrality }
				multiply_temp_variable = { NTR_united_north_num_bonus_divisions_temp_var = party_popularity@democratic }
			}
			
			divide_temp_variable = { NTR_united_north_num_bonus_divisions_temp_var = 3 }
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_template = "Tribal Garrison"
				}
				
				delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Tribal Garrison" } # fuck abusers
			}
			
			division_template = {
				name = "Tribal Garrison"
				is_locked = yes
				
				regiments = {
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
				}
				
				priority = 0
			}
			
			while_loop_effect = {
				limit = { always = yes } # do_while
				
				random_scope_in_array = {
					array = controlled_states
					
					limit = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
					}
					
					create_unit = { division = "name = \"Tribal Brigade\" division_template = \"Tribal Garrison\" start_experience_factor = 0.1 start_equipment_factor = 0.8" }
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { NTR_united_north_num_bonus_divisions_temp_var < 1 }
					}
					
					set_temp_variable = { break = 1 }
				}
				else = {
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { NTR_united_north_num_bonus_divisions_temp_var = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.534.t
	desc = Ntribes.534.d
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = democratic
			}
			
			neutrality > 0
		}
		else = {
			democratic > 0
		}
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = Ntribes.534.a
		
		custom_effect_tooltip = NTR_fight_for_our_homeland_tooltip
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_ideas = NTR_fight_for_our_homeland_idea
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # In the confrontation, we have benefited
	id = Ntribes.546
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.546"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_popularity_add_var = 0.06 } # 6% from all population_var
			set_temp_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_popularity_variation_temp_var = party_popularity@ruling_party }
			
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_popularity_variation_temp_var = 1 } # (-1~0) # reverse non-ruling support
			multiply_temp_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_popularity_variation_temp_var = -0.1 } # 10% from non-ruling supporters
			
			clamp_temp_variable = {
				var = NTR_unite_the_tribes_popularity_variation_temp_var
				max = 0.03 # max +- 3%
			}
			
			multiply_temp_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_popularity_variation_temp_var = random }
			
			random_list = {
				40 = {
					add_to_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_popularity_add_var = NTR_unite_the_tribes_popularity_variation_temp_var }
				}
				
				60 = {
					subtract_from_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_popularity_add_var = NTR_unite_the_tribes_popularity_variation_temp_var }
				}
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = var:NTR_unite_the_tribes_popularity_add_var
				}
			}
			
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = var:NTR_unite_the_tribes_popularity_add_var
				}
			}
			
			else = {
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = var:NTR_unite_the_tribes_popularity_add_var
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.546.t
	desc = Ntribes.546.d
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		name = Ntribes.546.a
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = var:NTR_unite_the_tribes_popularity_add_var
				}
			}
			
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = var:NTR_unite_the_tribes_popularity_add_var
				}
			}
			
			else = {
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = var:NTR_unite_the_tribes_popularity_add_var
				}
			}
		}
		
		clear_variable = NTR_unite_the_tribes_popularity_add_var
	}
}
