			set_temp_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_popularity_variation_temp_var = party_popularity@democratic }
			
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_popularity_variation_temp_var = 1 } # (-1~0) # reverse communism and neutrality support
			multiply_temp_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_popularity_variation_temp_var = -0.1 } # 10% from communism and neutrality supporters
			
			clamp_temp_variable = {
				var = NTR_unite_the_tribes_popularity_variation_temp_var
				max = 0.03 # max +- 3%
			}
			
			multiply_temp_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_popularity_variation_temp_var = random }
			
			random_list = {
				40 = {
					add_to_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_popularity_add_var = NTR_unite_the_tribes_popularity_variation_temp_var }
				}
				
				60 = {
					subtract_from_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_popularity_add_var = NTR_unite_the_tribes_popularity_variation_temp_var }
				}
			}
			
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = var:NTR_unite_the_tribes_popularity_add_var
			}
			
			set_temp_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_democratic_popularity_half_temp_var = party_popularity@democratic }
			multiply_temp_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_democratic_popularity_half_temp_var = 0.8 }
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							focus_progress = {
								focus = NTR_keep_what_is_ours
								progress > 0
							}
							
							focus_progress = {
								focus = NTR_use_guilds_savings
								progress > 0
							}
						}
					}
					
					check_variable = { NTR_harmonic_tribes_democratic_drift_var < 0.03 }
					check_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_democratic_popularity_half_temp_var > NTR_popularity_democratic_quarter }
				}
				
				add_to_variable = { NTR_harmonic_tribes_democratic_drift_var = 0.02 }
				
				set_country_flag = NTR_democrats_debuffs_increased
			}
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.547.t
	desc = Ntribes.547.d
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		name = Ntribes.547.a
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = var:NTR_unite_the_tribes_popularity_add_var
			}
		}
		
		clear_variable = NTR_unite_the_tribes_popularity_add_var
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = NTR_democrats_debuffs_increased
			}
			
			custom_effect_tooltip = NTR_democratic_influence_dynamic_modifier_increased_red_tooltip
			
			hidden_effect = {
				clr_country_flag = NTR_democrats_debuffs_increased
			}
		}
	}
}

				else = {
					add_political_power = 50
					add_stability = -0.025
					add_war_support = 0.025
					
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = democratic
						popularity = -0.05
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = neutrality
						popularity = 0.04
					}
					
					country_event = {
						id = Ntribes.552
						days = 6
						random = 48
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = NTR_ai_behavior
							option = VEDINA
						}
						
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = NTR_ai_behavior
							option = TRADE
						}
						
						has_country_flag = NTR_AI_VEDINA
						has_country_flag = NTR_AI_TRADE
					}
				}
				
				effect_tooltip = {
					add_political_power = 25
					add_stability = -0.025
					
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = democratic
						popularity = -0.025
					}
					
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = neutrality
						popularity = 0.025
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				effect_tooltip = {
					add_political_power = 50
					add_stability = -0.025
					add_war_support = 0.025
					
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = democratic
						popularity = -0.05
					}
					
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = neutrality
						popularity = 0.04
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

country_event = { # The Counterattack
	id = Ntribes.552
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.552"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_border_war_between = {
						attacker = 561
						defender = 677
					}
				}
				
				cancel_border_war = {
					dont_fire_events = yes
					defender = 677
					attacker = 561
				}
			}
			
			start_border_war = {
				change_state_after_war = no
				
				attacker = {
					state = 677
					num_provinces = 5
					on_win = Ntribes.553
					on_lose = Ntribes.554
					on_cancel = Ntribes.554
				}
				
				defender = {
					state = 561
					num_provinces = 6
					on_win = srs_borderwar.6
					on_lose = srs_borderwar.7
					on_cancel = srs_borderwar.5
				}
			}
			
			add_political_power = 25
			add_stability = -0.05
			
			677 = { add_manpower = -1340 }
			562 = { add_manpower = 860 }
			
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = -0.05
			}
			
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = Ntribes.553
					days = 3
					random = 24
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.552.t

				has_country_flag = NTR_AI_SYNTHESIS
			}
		}
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_political_power = -25
			add_stability = -0.05
			add_war_support = 0.025
			
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = 0.025
			}
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NTR_ai_behavior
						option = DEFAULT
					}
				}
				
				add_political_power = -25
				add_stability = -0.05
				add_war_support = 0.025
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = 0.025
				}
				
				country_event = {
					id = Ntribes.562
					days = 7
					random = 28
				}
			}
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Heads or Tails
		name = Ntribes.559.c
		
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = NTR_ai_behavior
					option = DEFAULT
				}
				
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = NTR_ai_behavior
					option = RANDOM
				}
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = NTR_ai_behavior
					option = DEFAULT
				}
			}
			
			custom_effect_tooltip = NTR_play_with_system_tooltip
			
			effect_tooltip = {
				random_list = {
					40 = {
						add_political_power = 25
					}
					
					60 = {
						add_political_power = -25
						add_stability = -0.05
						add_war_support = 0.025
						
						add_popularity = {
							ideology = neutrality
							popularity = 0.025
						}
					}
				}
			}
			
			hidden_effect = {
				NTR_calculate_political_path_if_necessary = yes
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = NTR_AI_VEDINA
							has_country_flag = NTR_AI_TRADE
						}
					}
					
					add_political_power = 25
					
					country_event = {
						id = Ntribes.560
						days = 14
						random = 56
					}
				}
				
				else = {
					add_stability = -0.025
					add_war_support = 0.025
					
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = neutrality
						popularity = 0.025
					}
					
					country_event = {
						id = Ntribes.562
						days = 7
						random = 28
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NTR_ai_behavior
						option = VEDINA
					}
					
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NTR_ai_behavior
						option = TRADE
					}
					
					has_country_flag = NTR_AI_VEDINA
					has_country_flag = NTR_AI_TRADE
				}
				
				effect_tooltip = {
					add_political_power = 25
				}
			}
			
			else = {
				effect_tooltip = {
					add_political_power = -25
					add_stability = -0.05
					add_war_support = 0.025
					
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = neutrality
						popularity = 0.025
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # The Tribes are Getting out of Control
	id = Ntribes.565
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.565"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			add_political_power = -50
			add_stability = -0.075
			add_war_support = -0.05
			
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = -0.075
			}
			
			add_to_variable = { NTR_traditionalism_influence_neutrality_drift_var = 0.01 }
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { NTR_communist_partisans_communism_drift_var < 0.08 }
				}
				
				add_to_variable = { NTR_communist_partisans_communism_drift_var = 0.01 }
			}
			
			NTR_set_demilitarized_zones = yes # to remove through on_actions #???
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_idea = disarmed_nation }
				}
				
				add_ideas = volunteer_only
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = NTR_ai_behavior
							option = DEFAULT
						}
					}
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_ai = no
						
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = NTR_ai_behavior
							option = RANDOM
						}
					}
					
					if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								has_country_flag = NTR_AI_TRADITIONS
								has_country_flag = NTR_AI_SYNTHESIS
							}
						}
						
						add_popularity = {
							ideology = neutrality
							popularity = 0.06
						}
						
						country_event = {
							id = Ntribes.566
							days = 14
							random = 56
						}
					}
					
					else = {
						add_political_power = -75
						
						add_popularity = {
							ideology = neutrality
							popularity = 0.04
						}
						
						country_event = {
							id = Ntribes.571
							days = 21
							random = 84
						}
					}
				}
				
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = NTR_AI_TRADITIONS
							has_country_flag = NTR_AI_SYNTHESIS
						}
					}
					
					add_stability = -0.025
					
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = neutrality
						popularity = 0.05
					}
					
					country_event = {
						id = Ntribes.566
						days = 14
						random = 56
					}
				}
				
				else = {
					add_political_power = -50
					add_stability = -0.025
					
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = neutrality
						popularity = 0.05
					}

						random = 84
					}

country_event = { # The Trial
	id = Ntribes.576
	
	immediate = { #???
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.576"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = -0.05
			}
			
			subtract_from_variable = { NTR_communist_partisans_communism_drift_var = 0.01 }
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = NTR_ai_behavior
							option = DEFAULT
						}
					}
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_ai = no
						
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = NTR_ai_behavior
							option = RANDOM
						}
					}
					
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_country_flag = NTR_AI_VEDINA
						}
						
						add_political_power = 100
						add_stability = 0.05
						
						add_popularity = {
							ideology = democratic
							popularity = 0.025
						}
					}
					
					else = {
						add_political_power = 150
						add_stability = 0.025
						
						add_popularity = {
							ideology = democratic
							popularity = 0.05
						}
						
						set_country_flag = NTR_SRS_more_peaceful_politics
					}
				}
				
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = NTR_AI_VEDINA
					}
					
					add_political_power = 75
					add_stability = 0.05
					
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = democratic
						popularity = 0.025
					}
				}
				
				else = {
					add_political_power = 125
					add_stability = 0.025
					
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = democratic
						popularity = 0.05
					}
					
					set_country_flag = NTR_SRS_more_peaceful_politics
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.576.t
	desc = Ntribes.576.d
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

				AND = {
					is_ai = no

						rule = NTR_ai_behavior
						option = DEFAULT
					}
				}
				
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = NTR_ai_behavior
					option = VEDINA
				}
				
				AND = {
					is_ai = yes
					
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NTR_ai_behavior
						option = RANDOM
					}
				}
				
				has_country_flag = NTR_AI_VEDINA
			}
		}
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_political_power = 75
			add_stability = 0.05
			
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = 0.025
			}
			
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = -0.05
			}
		}
		
		custom_effect_tooltip = NTR_communist_partisans_dynamic_modifier_reduced_green_tooltip
		
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NTR_ai_behavior
						option = DEFAULT
					}
				}
				
				add_political_power = 75
				add_stability = 0.05

					ideology = democratic
					popularity = 0.025

			}

				}
			}
		}
		
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NTR_AI_VEDINA
				}
				
				effect_tooltip = {
					add_political_power = 100
					add_stability = 0.05
					
					add_popularity = {

						popularity = 0.05

country_event = { # The Sudden Coup
	id = Ntribes.579
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.579"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { # -PP (-750 - -250)
					check_variable = { party_popularity@democratic > party_popularity@communism }
				}
				
				set_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_multiplier_temp_var = party_popularity@communism }
				divide_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_multiplier_temp_var = party_popularity@democratic }
				add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_multiplier_temp_var = -1 }
				
				set_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_temp_var = 500 }
			}
			else = { # +PP (-250 - +250)
				set_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_multiplier_temp_var = party_popularity@democratic }
				divide_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_multiplier_temp_var = party_popularity@communism }
				add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_multiplier_temp_var = -1 }
				
				set_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_temp_var = -500 }
			}
			
			multiply_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_temp_var = NTR_political_power_after_coup_multiplier_temp_var }
			add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_temp_var = -250 }
			add_political_power = NTR_political_power_after_coup_temp_var
			
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = communism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = 0.075
			}
			
			# slots swap
			remove_ideas = NTR_ivor_eklund
			
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = NTR_adam_watershed
				add_idea = NTR_ivor_eklund
			}
			
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NTR_communist_partisans_dynamic_modifier }
			clear_variable = NTR_communist_partisans_communism_drift_var
			
			remove_ideas = NTR_communist_partisans_idea
			
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Adam Watershed" # Chairman of General National Congress
				desc = ""
				picture = "Governor.tga" # portrait #???
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = leninism
				traits = { national_hero }
			}
			
			create_corps_commander = {
				name = "Adam Watershed"
				picture = "Governor.tga" # portrait #???
				id = 13457
				skill = 3
				attack_skill = 3
				defense_skill = 2
				planning_skill = 2
				logistics_skill = 3
				traits = { war_hero tribal_warchief organizer winter_specialist }
			}
			
			create_corps_commander = { # to advisor someday #???
				name = "Ivor Eklund"
				picture = "Blind_archer.tga"
				id = 13458
				skill = 2
				attack_skill = 1
				defense_skill = 3
				planning_skill = 1
				logistics_skill = 2
				traits = { blind war_hero tribal_warchief adaptable winter_specialist }
			}
			
			set_variable = { NTR_harmonic_tribes_democratic_drift_var = 0.04 }
			add_NTR_harmonic_tribes_dynamic_modifier_effects = yes
			
			add_ideas = NTR_harmonic_tribes_idea
			
			log = "[This.GetName]: self-triggering event Ntribes.597 started"
			country_event = { id = Ntribes.597 days = 1 }
			
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = export_focus
				add_idea = limited_exports
			}
			
			random_unit_leader = {
				limit = {
					has_id = 13450
				}
				
				set_nationality = SOL
			}
			
			NTR_remove_demilitarized_zones = yes
			
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = SRS.core_states
				
				remove_claim_by = ROOT
			}
			
			set_cosmetic_tag = NTR_SRS_faction
			
			country_event = Ntribes.596
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.579.t
	desc = Ntribes.579.d
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { # The Red Banner Rises in the North
		name = Ntribes.579.a
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = communism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = 0.075
			}
			
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Adam Watershed" # Chairman of General National Congress
				desc = ""
				picture = "Governor.tga" # portrait #???
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = leninism
				traits = { national_hero }
			}
			
			create_corps_commander = {

				logistics_skill = 3

			}

country_event = { # The Tribal Council Makes its Move
	id = Ntribes.581
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.581"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { # -PP (-750 - -250)
					check_variable = { party_popularity@democratic > party_popularity@neutrality }
				}
				
				set_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_multiplier_temp_var = party_popularity@neutrality }
				divide_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_multiplier_temp_var = party_popularity@democratic }
				add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_multiplier_temp_var = -1 }
				
				set_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_temp_var = 500 }
			}
			else = { # +PP (-250 - +250)
				set_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_multiplier_temp_var = party_popularity@democratic }
				divide_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_multiplier_temp_var = party_popularity@neutrality }
				add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_multiplier_temp_var = -1 }
				
				set_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_temp_var = -500 }
			}
			
			multiply_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_temp_var = NTR_political_power_after_coup_multiplier_temp_var }
			add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_temp_var = -250 }
			add_political_power = NTR_political_power_after_coup_temp_var
			
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = 0.05
			}
			
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = export_focus
				add_idea = limited_exports
			}
			
			set_variable = { NTR_harmonic_tribes_democratic_drift_var = 0.04 }
			add_NTR_harmonic_tribes_dynamic_modifier_effects = yes
			
			add_ideas = NTR_harmonic_tribes_idea
			
			log = "[This.GetName]: self-triggering event Ntribes.597 started"
			country_event = { id = Ntribes.597 days = 1 }
			
			subtract_from_variable = { NTR_communist_partisans_communism_drift_var = 0.02 }
			
			random_unit_leader = {
				limit = {
					has_id = 13450
				}
				
				set_nationality = SOL
			}
			
			NTR_remove_demilitarized_zones = yes
			
			load_focus_tree = {
				tree = NTR_tribal_council_basic_focus_tree
				keep_completed = yes
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_rule = can_guarantee_other_ideologies
				}
				
				set_rule = { can_guarantee_other_ideologies = no }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_rule = can_boost_other_ideologies
				}
				
				set_rule = { can_boost_other_ideologies = no }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_rule = can_send_volunteers
				}
				
				set_rule = { can_send_volunteers = no }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_rule = can_create_factions
				}
				
				set_rule = { can_create_factions = no }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_rule = can_join_factions
				}
				
				set_rule = { can_join_factions = no }
			}
			
			set_country_flag = NTR_neutrality_rules #???
			
			country_event = Ntribes.596
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.581.t
	desc = Ntribes.581.d
	#picture =

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { # We remember who we are

			}

				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = 0.05
			}
			
			add_ideas = NTR_harmonic_tribes_idea
			
			remove_ideas = NTR_adam_watershed
			remove_ideas = NTR_ivor_eklund
			
			custom_effect_tooltip = NTR_communist_partisans_dynamic_modifier_reduced_green_tooltip
			
			remove_unit_leader = 13450
			
			set_rule = {
				can_guarantee_other_ideologies = no
				can_boost_other_ideologies = no
				can_send_volunteers = no
				can_create_factions = no
				can_join_factions = no

		}

country_event = { #	Check for decreasing of the ideological ideas
	id = Ntribes.588
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.588" }
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = democratic
			}
			
			set_temp_variable = { NTR_reintegration_half_temp_var = party_popularity@neutrality }
			add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_reintegration_half_temp_var = party_popularity@communism }
			
			set_temp_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_neutrality_popularity_two_thirds_temp_var = party_popularity@neutrality }
			multiply_temp_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_neutrality_popularity_two_thirds_temp_var = 0.67 }
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = NTR_unite_the_tribes_neutrality_popularity_two_thirds_temp_var
						compare = less_than_or_equals
						value = NTR_popularity_neutrality_two_thirds
					}
				}
				
				country_event = Ntribes.541
			}
			
			divide_temp_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_neutrality_popularity_two_thirds_temp_var = 2 }
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = NTR_unite_the_tribes_neutrality_popularity_two_thirds_temp_var
						compare = less_than_or_equals
						value = NTR_popularity_neutrality_thirds
					}
				}
				
				country_event = Ntribes.540
			}
			
			set_temp_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_communism_popularity_quarter_temp_var = party_popularity@communism }
			divide_temp_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_communism_popularity_quarter_temp_var = 2 }
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = NTR_unite_the_tribes_communism_popularity_quarter_temp_var
						compare = less_than_or_equals
						value = NTR_popularity_communism_quarter
					}
				}
				
				random_owned_controlled_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
						
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								state = 574
								state = 677
							}
						}
					}
					
					set_variable = { PREV.NTR_communist_headquarters_state = THIS }
				}
				
				country_event = Ntribes.539
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = yes
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						communism < 0.05
					}
					
					activate_decision = NTR_the_last_communist_stronghold
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						neutrality < 0.05
					}
					
					activate_decision = NTR_breaking_the_tribal_council
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						democratic > 0.6
					}
					
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { party_popularity@communism > party_popularity@neutrality }
						}
						
						activate_decision = NTR_offer_amnesty_to_communists
					}
					else = {
						activate_decision = NTR_take_the_tribal_council_to_task
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						democratic > 0.4
						
						communism > 0.15
						neutrality > 0.15
					}
					
					set_temp_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_reversed_ruling_party_support_temp_var = 1 }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_reversed_ruling_party_support_temp_var = party_popularity@ruling_party }
					
					random_list = {
						50 = {
							modifier = {
								factor = NTR_unite_the_tribes_reversed_ruling_party_support_temp_var
								
								has_variable = NTR_unite_the_tribes_reversed_ruling_party_support_temp_var
							}
							
							activate_decision = NTR_play_the_tribal_council_and_the_communists_against_each_other
						}
						50 = {
							activate_decision = NTR_the_advantages_of_free_trade
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					activate_decision = NTR_the_advantages_of_free_trade
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = communism
			}
			
			set_temp_variable = { NTR_reintegration_half_temp_var = party_popularity@neutrality }
			add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_reintegration_half_temp_var = party_popularity@democratic }
			
			set_temp_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_neutrality_popularity_two_thirds_temp_var = party_popularity@neutrality }
			multiply_temp_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_neutrality_popularity_two_thirds_temp_var = 0.67 }
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = NTR_popularity_neutrality_two_thirds
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							var = NTR_unite_the_tribes_neutrality_popularity_two_thirds_temp_var
							compare = less_than_or_equals
							value = NTR_popularity_neutrality_two_thirds
						}
					}
					
					country_event = Ntribes.541
				}
			}
			
			divide_temp_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_neutrality_popularity_two_thirds_temp_var = 2 }
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = NTR_unite_the_tribes_neutrality_popularity_two_thirds_temp_var
						compare = less_than_or_equals
						value = NTR_popularity_neutrality_thirds
					}
				}
				
				country_event = Ntribes.540
			}
			
			set_temp_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_democratic_popularity_quarter_temp_var = party_popularity@democratic }
			divide_temp_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_democratic_popularity_quarter_temp_var = 2 }
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = NTR_unite_the_tribes_democratic_popularity_quarter_temp_var
						compare = less_than_or_equals
						value = NTR_popularity_democratic_quarter
					}
				}
				
				country_event = Ntribes.538
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = yes
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						democratic < 0.05
					}
					
					activate_decision = NTR_do_away_with_the_snowflakes
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						neutrality < 0.05
					}
					
					activate_decision = NTR_breaking_the_tribal_council
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						communism > 0.6
					}
					
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { party_popularity@democratic > party_popularity@neutrality }
						}
						
						activate_decision = NTR_dealing_with_fianas_supporters
					}
					else = {
						activate_decision = NTR_take_the_tribal_council_to_task
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						communism > 0.4
						
						democratic > 0.15
						neutrality > 0.15
					}
					
					set_temp_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_reversed_ruling_party_support_temp_var = 1 }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_reversed_ruling_party_support_temp_var = party_popularity@ruling_party }
					
					random_list = {

							modifier = {
								factor = NTR_unite_the_tribes_reversed_ruling_party_support_temp_var
								
								has_variable = NTR_unite_the_tribes_reversed_ruling_party_support_temp_var
							}
							
							activate_decision = NTR_bait_the_tribal_council
						}
						50 = {
							activate_decision = NTR_revolutionary_education_for_the_masses
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					activate_decision = NTR_revolutionary_education_for_the_masses
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { NTR_reintegration_half_temp_var = party_popularity@democratic }
			add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_reintegration_half_temp_var = party_popularity@communism }
			
			set_temp_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_democratic_popularity_quarter_temp_var = party_popularity@democratic }
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = NTR_unite_the_tribes_democratic_popularity_quarter_temp_var
						compare = less_than_or_equals
						value = NTR_popularity_democratic_quarter
					}
				}
				
				country_event = Ntribes.538
			}
			
			set_temp_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_communism_popularity_quarter_temp_var = party_popularity@communism }
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = NTR_unite_the_tribes_communism_popularity_quarter_temp_var
						compare = less_than_or_equals
						value = NTR_popularity_communism_quarter
					}
				}
				
				random_owned_controlled_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
						
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								state = 574
								state = 677
							}
						}
					}
					
					set_variable = { PREV.NTR_communist_headquarters_state = THIS }
				}
				
				country_event = Ntribes.539
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = yes
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						democratic < 0.05
					}
					
					activate_decision = NTR_do_away_with_the_snowflakes
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						communism < 0.05
					}
					
					activate_decision = NTR_the_last_communist_stronghold
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						neutrality > 0.6
					}
					
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { party_popularity@communism > party_popularity@democratic }
						}
						
						activate_decision = NTR_offer_amnesty_to_communists
					}
					else = {
						activate_decision = NTR_dealing_with_fianas_supporters
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						neutrality > 0.4
						
						communism > 0.15
						democratic > 0.15
					}
					
					set_temp_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_reversed_ruling_party_support_temp_var = 1 }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_reversed_ruling_party_support_temp_var = party_popularity@ruling_party }
					
					random_list = {
						50 = {
							modifier = {
								factor = NTR_unite_the_tribes_reversed_ruling_party_support_temp_var
								
								has_variable = NTR_unite_the_tribes_reversed_ruling_party_support_temp_var
							}
							
							activate_decision = NTR_unite_under_one_banner_by_force_or_diplomacy
						}
						50 = {
							activate_decision = NTR_millennial_traditions
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					activate_decision = NTR_millennial_traditions
				}
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = NTR_reintegration_half_temp_var
					compare = less_than_or_equals
					value = NTR_reintegration_half
				}
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_government = neutrality }
				}
				
				country_event = Ntribes.545
			}
			else = {
				country_event = Ntribes.544
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { NTR_reintegration_half_temp_var < 0.1 }
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_government = neutrality }
				}
				
				country_event = Ntribes.543
			}
			else = {
				country_event = Ntribes.542
			}
		}
	}
}

	fire_only_once = no

country_event = { # Check for calling anti-government events
	id = Ntribes.595
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.595" }
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = NTR_integration_in_process_flag
	}
	
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { party_popularity@ruling_party > 0.4 }
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				
				random_list = {
					30 = { # neu+
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							
							OR = {
								check_variable = { party_popularity@neutrality = 0 }
								
								AND = {
									focus_progress = {
										focus = NTR_new_regional_administration
										progress > 0
									}
									NOT = { has_completed_focus = NTR_new_regional_administration }
								}
							}
						}
						
						country_event = Ntribes.549
					}
					
					30 = { # com+
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							
							OR = {
								check_variable = { party_popularity@communism = 0 }
								
								AND = {
									focus_progress = {
										focus = NTR_guilds_will_do_their_part
										progress > 0
									}
									NOT = { has_completed_focus = NTR_guilds_will_do_their_part }
								}
							}
						}
						
						country_event = Ntribes.548
					}
					
					40 = {
						modifier = {
							add = -10
							
							check_variable = { party_popularity@ruling_party > 0.6 }
						}
						modifier = {
							add = -10
							
							check_variable = { party_popularity@ruling_party > 0.8 }
						}
						
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							
							OR = {
								check_variable = { party_popularity@neutrality = 0 }
								check_variable = { party_popularity@communism = 0 }
							}
						}
						
						set_temp_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_ruling_party_multiplier_temp_var = 1 }
						subtract_from_temp_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_ruling_party_multiplier_temp_var = party_popularity@ruling_party }
						
						set_temp_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_ruling_party_ratio_temp_var = 1 }
						divide_temp_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_ruling_party_ratio_temp_var = NTR_unite_the_tribes_ruling_party_multiplier_temp_var }
						multiply_temp_variable = { NTR_unite_the_tribes_ruling_party_ratio_temp_var = 10 }
						
						set_variable = { NTR_communism_emergency_support = party_popularity@communism }
						multiply_variable = { NTR_communism_emergency_support = NTR_unite_the_tribes_ruling_party_multiplier_temp_var }
						round_variable = NTR_communism_emergency_support
						
						set_variable = { NTR_neutrality_emergency_support = party_popularity@neutrality }
						divide_variable = { NTR_neutrality_emergency_support = NTR_unite_the_tribes_ruling_party_multiplier_temp_var }
						round_variable = NTR_neutrality_emergency_support
						
						activate_mission = NTR_clashes_in_the_north
						
						if = {
							limit = {
								is_ai = yes
							}
							
							if = {
								limit = {
									check_variable = { party_popularity@communism > party_popularity@neutrality }
								}
								
								activate_decision = NTR_strike_the_communists
							}
							else = {
								activate_decision = NTR_strike_the_neutrals
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				
				random_list = {
					30 = { # neu+
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							
							OR = {
								check_variable = { party_popularity@neutrality = 0 }
								
								AND = {
									focus_progress = {
										focus = NTR_transforming_the_old_traditions
										progress > 0
									}
									NOT = { has_completed_focus = NTR_transforming_the_old_traditions }
								}
							}
						}
						
						country_event = Ntribes.549
					}
					
					30 = { # dem+
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							
							OR = {
								check_variable = { party_popularity@democratic = 0 }
								
								AND = {
									focus_progress = {
										focus = NTR_transforming_the_old_traditions
										progress > 0
									}
									NOT = { has_completed_focus = NTR_use_guilds_savings }
								}
							}
						}
						
						country_event = Ntribes.547
					}
					
					40 = {
						modifier = {
							add = -10
							
							check_variable = { party_popularity@ruling_party > 0.6 }
						}
						modifier = {
							add = -10
							
							check_variable = { party_popularity@ruling_party > 0.8 }
						}
						
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							
							OR = {
								check_variable = { party_popularity@neutrality = 0 }
								check_variable = { party_popularity@democratic = 0 }
							}
						}
						
						set_variable = { NTR_democratic_emergency_support = party_popularity@democratic }
						divide_variable = { NTR_democratic_emergency_support = party_popularity@neutrality }
						
						set_variable = { NTR_neutrality_emergency_support = party_popularity@neutrality }
						divide_variable = { NTR_neutrality_emergency_support = party_popularity@democratic }
						
						activate_mission = NTR_clashes_in_the_north
						
						if = {
							limit = {
								is_ai = yes
							}
							
							if = {
								limit = {
									check_variable = { party_popularity@democratic > party_popularity@neutrality }
								}
								
								activate_decision = NTR_strike_the_democrats
							}
							else = {
								activate_decision = NTR_strike_the_neutrals
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_list = {
					30 = { # com+
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							
							OR = {
								check_variable = { party_popularity@communism = 0 }
								
								AND = {
									focus_progress = {
										focus = NTR_reasserting_tribal_authority
										progress > 0
									}
									NOT = { has_completed_focus = NTR_reasserting_tribal_authority }
								}
							}
						}
						
						country_event = Ntribes.548
					}
					
					30 = { # dem+
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							
							OR = {
								check_variable = { party_popularity@democratic = 0 }
								
								AND = {
									focus_progress = {
										focus = NTR_keep_what_is_ours
										progress > 0
									}
									NOT = { has_completed_focus = NTR_keep_what_is_ours }
								}
							}
						}
						
						country_event = Ntribes.547
					}
					
					40 = {
						modifier = {
							add = -10
							
							check_variable = { party_popularity@ruling_party > 0.6 }
						}
						modifier = {
							add = -10
							
							check_variable = { party_popularity@ruling_party > 0.8 }
						}
						
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							
							OR = {
								check_variable = { party_popularity@communism = 0 }
								check_variable = { party_popularity@democratic = 0 }
							}
						}
						
						set_variable = { NTR_communism_emergency_support = party_popularity@communism }
						divide_variable = { NTR_communism_emergency_support = party_popularity@democratic }
						
						set_variable = { NTR_democratic_emergency_support = party_popularity@democratic }
						divide_variable = { NTR_democratic_emergency_support = party_popularity@communism }
						
						activate_mission = NTR_clashes_in_the_north
						
						if = {
							limit = {
								is_ai = yes
							}
							
							if = {
								limit = {
									check_variable = { party_popularity@communism > party_popularity@democratic }
								}
								
								activate_decision = NTR_strike_the_communists
							}
							else = {
								activate_decision = NTR_strike_the_democrats
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		country_event = {
			id = Ntribes.595
			days = 45 # 45-60
			random = 360
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #	Calculation of variables for reintegration
	id = Ntribes.596
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.596" }
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		set_country_flag = NTR_integration_in_process_flag
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = democratic
			}
			
			set_variable = { NTR_popularity_neutrality_two_thirds = party_popularity@neutrality }
			multiply_variable = { NTR_popularity_neutrality_two_thirds = 0.667 }
			
			set_variable = { NTR_reintegration_half = party_popularity@neutrality }
			divide_variable = { NTR_reintegration_half = 2 }
			
			set_variable = { NTR_popularity_neutrality_thirds = NTR_popularity_neutrality_two_thirds }
			divide_variable = { NTR_popularity_neutrality_thirds = 2 }
			
			set_variable = { NTR_popularity_communism_quarter = party_popularity@communism }
			divide_variable = { NTR_popularity_communism_quarter = 2 }
			
			add_to_variable = { NTR_reintegration_half = NTR_popularity_communism_quarter }
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = yes
				}
				
				activate_decision = NTR_the_advantages_of_free_trade
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = communism
			}
			
			set_variable = { NTR_popularity_neutrality_two_thirds = party_popularity@neutrality }
			multiply_variable = { NTR_popularity_neutrality_two_thirds = 0.667 }
			
			set_variable = { NTR_reintegration_half = party_popularity@neutrality }
			divide_variable = { NTR_reintegration_half = 2 }
			
			set_variable = { NTR_popularity_neutrality_thirds = NTR_popularity_neutrality_two_thirds }
			divide_variable = { NTR_popularity_neutrality_thirds = 2 }
			
			set_variable = { NTR_popularity_democratic_quarter = party_popularity@democratic }
			divide_variable = { NTR_popularity_democratic_quarter = 2 }
			
			add_to_variable = { NTR_reintegration_half = NTR_popularity_democratic_quarter }
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = yes
				}
				
				activate_decision = NTR_revolutionary_education_for_the_masses
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_variable = { NTR_popularity_democratic_quarter = party_popularity@democratic }
			divide_variable = { NTR_popularity_democratic_quarter = 2 }
			
			set_variable = { NTR_reintegration_half = NTR_popularity_democratic_quarter }
			
			set_variable = { NTR_popularity_communism_quarter = party_popularity@communism }
			divide_variable = { NTR_popularity_communism_quarter = 2 }
			
			add_to_variable = { NTR_reintegration_half = NTR_popularity_communism_quarter }
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = yes
				}
				
				activate_decision = NTR_millennial_traditions
			}
		}
		
		country_event = {
			id = Ntribes.595
			days = 45
			random = 360
		}
	}
}

	id = Ntribes.597

		}

country_event = { # Refugees from the East
	id = Ntribes.908
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.908"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			add_stability = -0.05
			
			set_variable = { divider = -10 }
			set_variable = { randomizer = 0.3 }
			set_variable = { rounder = 100 }
			
			DED = { save_current_manpower = yes }
			
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 565
						state = 566
						state = 428
					}
				}
				
				set_variable = { population_var = state_population }
				population_calculator_multifunctional = yes
				population_calculation_for_sum = yes
			}
			
			DED = { restore_previous_manpower = yes }
			
			multiply_variable = { population_sum = -1 }
			
			set_variable = { divider = 2 }
			set_variable = { randomizer = 0.2 }
			set_variable = { rounder = 100 }
			
			set_variable = { population_var = population_sum }
			population_calculator_multifunctional = yes
			subtract_from_variable = { population_sum = population_var }
			
			population_calculator_cleaner = yes
			
			save_current_manpower = yes
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { population_sum > population_var }
				}
				
				573 = { add_manpower = ROOT.population_sum }
				563 = { add_manpower = ROOT.population_var }
			}
			else = {
				573 = { add_manpower = ROOT.population_var }
				563 = { add_manpower = ROOT.population_sum }
			}
			
			restore_previous_manpower = yes
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.908.t
	desc = Ntribes.908.d
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { # Send healers and food east to help however we can
		name = Ntribes.908.a
		
		trigger = {
			has_government = democratic
		}
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_stability = -0.05
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { population_sum > population_var }
				}
				
				573 = { add_manpower = ROOT.population_sum }
				563 = { add_manpower = ROOT.population_var }
			}
			else = {
				573 = { add_manpower = ROOT.population_var }
				563 = { add_manpower = ROOT.population_sum }
			}
		}
		
		population_clr_junk = yes
		
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = Ntribes.909
				days = 3
				random = 24
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # They are welcome here
		name = Ntribes.908.b
		
		trigger = {
			has_government = communism
		}
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_stability = -0.05
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { population_sum > population_var }
				}
				
				573 = { add_manpower = ROOT.population_sum }
				563 = { add_manpower = ROOT.population_var }
			}
			else = {
				573 = { add_manpower = ROOT.population_var }
				563 = { add_manpower = ROOT.population_sum }
			}
		}
		
		population_clr_junk = yes
		
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = Ntribes.909
				days = 3
				random = 24
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Find out what has happened

		trigger = {
			has_government = neutrality
		}
		
		effect_tooltip = {

country_event = { # Remove effects from Ntribes.989
	id = Ntribes.988
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.988" }
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NTR_griffon_race_technologies_upkeep_modifier }
			}
			
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NTR_griffon_race_technologies_upkeep_modifier }
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = NTR_griffon_race_technologies_upkeep_5RS_idea
			}
			
			remove_ideas = NTR_griffon_race_technologies_upkeep_5RS_idea
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = NTR_griffon_race_technologies_upkeep_4RS_idea
			}
			
			remove_ideas = NTR_griffon_race_technologies_upkeep_4RS_idea
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = NTR_griffon_race_technologies_upkeep_3RS_idea
			}
			
			remove_ideas = NTR_griffon_race_technologies_upkeep_3RS_idea
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = NTR_griffon_race_technologies_upkeep_2RS_idea
			}
			
			remove_ideas = NTR_griffon_race_technologies_upkeep_2RS_idea
		}
		else = {
			remove_ideas = NTR_griffon_race_technologies_upkeep_1RS_idea
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Recalculation for NTR_griffon_race_technologies_category upkeep modifier
	id = Ntribes.989
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = NTR_griffon_race_technologies_cooldown
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { amount_research_slots > 4 }
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_idea = NTR_griffon_race_technologies_upkeep_5RS_idea }
					}
					
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_idea = NTR_griffon_race_technologies_upkeep_4RS_idea
						}
						
						swap_ideas = {
							remove_idea = NTR_griffon_race_technologies_upkeep_4RS_idea
							add_idea = NTR_griffon_race_technologies_upkeep_5RS_idea
						}
					}
					else = {
						add_ideas = NTR_griffon_race_technologies_upkeep_5RS_idea
					}
					
					adjust_research_modifier = yes
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { amount_research_slots > 3 }
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_idea = NTR_griffon_race_technologies_upkeep_4RS_idea }
					}
					
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_idea = NTR_griffon_race_technologies_upkeep_3RS_idea
						}
						
						swap_ideas = {
							remove_idea = NTR_griffon_race_technologies_upkeep_3RS_idea
							add_idea = NTR_griffon_race_technologies_upkeep_4RS_idea
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							has_idea = NTR_griffon_race_technologies_upkeep_5RS_idea
						}
						
						swap_ideas = {
							remove_idea = NTR_griffon_race_technologies_upkeep_5RS_idea
							add_idea = NTR_griffon_race_technologies_upkeep_4RS_idea
						}
					}
					else = {
						add_ideas = NTR_griffon_race_technologies_upkeep_4RS_idea
					}
					
					adjust_research_modifier = yes
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { amount_research_slots > 2 }
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_idea = NTR_griffon_race_technologies_upkeep_3RS_idea }
					}
					
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_idea = NTR_griffon_race_technologies_upkeep_2RS_idea
						}
						
						swap_ideas = {
							remove_idea = NTR_griffon_race_technologies_upkeep_2RS_idea
							add_idea = NTR_griffon_race_technologies_upkeep_3RS_idea
						}
					}
					else = {
						add_ideas = NTR_griffon_race_technologies_upkeep_3RS_idea
					}
					
					adjust_research_modifier = yes
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { amount_research_slots > 1 }
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_idea = NTR_griffon_race_technologies_upkeep_2RS_idea }
					}
					
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_idea = NTR_griffon_race_technologies_upkeep_1RS_idea
						}
						
						swap_ideas = {
							remove_idea = NTR_griffon_race_technologies_upkeep_1RS_idea
							add_idea = NTR_griffon_race_technologies_upkeep_2RS_idea
						}
					}
					else = {
						add_ideas = NTR_griffon_race_technologies_upkeep_2RS_idea
					}
					
					adjust_research_modifier = yes
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = NTR_griffon_race_technologies_upkeep_1RS_idea
				
				adjust_research_modifier = yes
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NTR_griffon_race_technologies_upkeep_modifier }
				}
				
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NTR_griffon_race_technologies_upkeep_modifier }
			}
			
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NTR_griffon_race_technologies_upkeep_modifier }
			
			country_event = {
				id = Ntribes.989
				days = 1
			}
		}
		else = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: self-triggering event Ntribes.989 stopped"
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Recalculation of upkeep variable for NTR_griffon_race_technologies_category
	id = Ntribes.990
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_government = fascism }
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = NTR_research_speed_factor_check
						compare = not_equals
						value = modifier@research_speed_factor
					}
				}
				
				set_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_griffons_upkeep_multiplier_temp_var = 1 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_griffons_upkeep_multiplier_temp_var = modifier@research_speed_factor }
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { modifier@research_speed_factor > 0 }
					}
					
					set_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_griffons_upkeep_reverser_temp_var = NTR_political_power_griffons_upkeep_multiplier_temp_var }
					multiply_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_griffons_upkeep_reverser_temp_var = NTR_political_power_griffons_upkeep_multiplier_temp_var }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { modifier@research_speed_factor < 0 }
					}
					
					set_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_griffons_upkeep_reverser_temp_var = 1 }
					divide_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_griffons_upkeep_reverser_temp_var = NTR_political_power_griffons_upkeep_multiplier_temp_var }
				}
				
				divide_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_griffons_upkeep_multiplier_temp_var = NTR_political_power_griffons_upkeep_reverser_temp_var }
				
				set_variable = { NTR_griffon_race_technologies_political_power_upkeep_var = -0.25 }
				multiply_variable = { NTR_griffon_race_technologies_political_power_upkeep_var = NTR_political_power_griffons_upkeep_multiplier_temp_var }
				
				set_variable = { NTR_research_speed_factor_check = modifier@research_speed_factor }
			}
			else = {
				set_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_griffons_upkeep_multiplier_temp_var = 1 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_griffons_upkeep_multiplier_temp_var = modifier@research_speed_factor }
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { modifier@research_speed_factor > 0 }
					}
					
					set_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_griffons_upkeep_reverser_temp_var = NTR_political_power_griffons_upkeep_multiplier_temp_var }
					multiply_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_griffons_upkeep_reverser_temp_var = NTR_political_power_griffons_upkeep_multiplier_temp_var }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { modifier@research_speed_factor < 0 }
					}
					
					set_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_griffons_upkeep_reverser_temp_var = 1 }
					divide_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_griffons_upkeep_reverser_temp_var = NTR_political_power_griffons_upkeep_multiplier_temp_var }
				}
				
				divide_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_griffons_upkeep_multiplier_temp_var = NTR_political_power_griffons_upkeep_reverser_temp_var }
				
				set_variable = { NTR_griffon_race_technologies_political_power_upkeep_var = -0.25 }
				multiply_variable = { NTR_griffon_race_technologies_political_power_upkeep_var = NTR_political_power_griffons_upkeep_multiplier_temp_var }
			}
			
			country_event = {
				id = Ntribes.990
				days = 1
			}
		}
		
		else = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: self-triggering event Ntribes.990 stopped"
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Self-triggering check for frozen_seas_dynamic_modifier with icebreakers_technology
	id = Ntribes.992
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = frozen_seas_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = frozen_seas_dynamic_modifier }
			
			set_variable = { NTR_icebreakers_required = modifier@min_export }
			multiply_variable = { NTR_icebreakers_required = 20 }
			
			set_temp_variable = { NTR_resources_temp_var = resource_exported@oil }
			add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_resources_temp_var = resource_exported@aluminium }
			add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_resources_temp_var = resource_exported@rubber }
			add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_resources_temp_var = resource_exported@tungsten }
			add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_resources_temp_var = resource_exported@steel }
			add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_resources_temp_var = resource_exported@chromium }
			add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_resources_temp_var = resource_exported@crystals }
			
			add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_resources_temp_var = resource_imported@oil }
			add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_resources_temp_var = resource_imported@aluminium }
			add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_resources_temp_var = resource_imported@rubber }
			add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_resources_temp_var = resource_imported@tungsten }
			add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_resources_temp_var = resource_imported@steel }
			add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_resources_temp_var = resource_imported@chromium }
			add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_resources_temp_var = resource_imported@crystals }
			
			divide_temp_variable = { NTR_resources_temp_var = 8 }
			round_temp_variable = NTR_resources_temp_var
			
			add_to_variable = { NTR_icebreakers_required = NTR_resources_temp_var }
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_decision = NTR_FAT_FAW_Tspirit
				}
				
				add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_icebreakers_for_agreements_neighbors_temp_var = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_decision = NTR_MNC_Tspirit
				}
				
				add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_icebreakers_for_agreements_neighbors_temp_var = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_decision = NTR_HLR_Tspirit
				}
				
				add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_icebreakers_for_agreements_neighbors_temp_var = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_decision = NTR_VED_Tspirit
				}
				
				add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_icebreakers_for_agreements_neighbors_temp_var = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_decision = NTR_PNG_Tspirit
				}
				
				add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_icebreakers_for_agreements_neighbors_temp_var = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_decision = NTR_NCH_Tspirit
				}
				
				add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_icebreakers_for_agreements_neighbors_temp_var = 1 }
			}
			
			multiply_temp_variable = { NTR_icebreakers_for_agreements_neighbors_temp_var = 3 }
			add_to_variable = { NTR_icebreakers_required = NTR_icebreakers_for_agreements_neighbors_temp_var }
			
			every_other_country = { # array? #???
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NTR_friends_check_for_bonus_dockyards
					
					exists = yes
					has_government = democratic
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_subject = no
					}
					
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_major = yes
						}
						
						add_to_variable = { ROOT.NTR_icebreakers_required = 3 }
					}
					else = {
						add_to_variable = { ROOT.NTR_icebreakers_required = 2 }
					}
				}
				else = {
					add_to_variable = { ROOT.NTR_icebreakers_required = 1 }
				}
			}
			
			round_variable = NTR_icebreakers_required
			
			set_variable = { NTR_icebreakers_reverse_ratio = num_equipment@icebreaker }
			divide_variable = { NTR_icebreakers_reverse_ratio = NTR_icebreakers_required }
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { NTR_icebreakers_reverse_ratio < 1 }
				}
				
				multiply_variable = { NTR_icebreakers_reverse_ratio = -1 }
				add_to_variable = { NTR_icebreakers_reverse_ratio = 1 }
				
				add_frozen_seas_dynamic_modifier_effects = yes
			}
			else = {
				set_variable = { var_frozen_seas_factory_capacity_debuff = 0 }
				set_variable = { var_frozen_seas_dockyard_capacity_debuff = 0 }
				set_variable = { var_frozen_seas_buildings_speed_debuff = 0 }
				set_variable = { var_frozen_seas_research_speed_debuff = 0 }
				set_variable = { var_frozen_seas_trade_opinion_debuff = 0 }
				set_variable = { var_frozen_seas_min_export_debuff = 0 }
				
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = frozen_seas_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			
			country_event = {
				id = Ntribes.992
				days = 7
			}
		}
		else = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: self-triggering event Ntribes.992 stopped"
		}
	}
}

		##########
		 # ROOT #
		##########
		
		if = { # pre-check for army AI behavior
			limit = {
				check_variable = { NTR_army_AI_factor < 3 } # value can be specified for every country (now only for NTR)
			}
			
			############
			 # At War #
			############
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_war = yes
				}
				
				if = { # check for neighborhood
					limit = {
						any_of_scopes = {
							array = enemies
							
							OR = {
								is_in_array = { ROOT.neighbors = THIS }
								
								any_of_scopes = {
									array = allies
									
									is_in_array = { ROOT.neighbors = THIS }
								}
								
								any_of_scopes = {
									array = ROOT.allies
									
									OR = {
										is_in_array = { PREV.neighbors = THIS }
										
										any_of_scopes = {
											array = PREV.allies
											
											is_in_array = { PREV.neighbors = THIS }
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					
					set_variable = { NTR_army_AI_factor = 3 } # land war
				}
				else = { # check for land connection
					for_each_scope_loop = {
						array = enemies
						
						for_each_scope_loop = {
							array = ROOT.neighbors
							
							if = {
								limit = {
									NOT = { is_in_array = { ROOT.allies = THIS } }
								}
								
								add_to_array = { PREV.possible_route = THIS }
							}
						}
						
						for_each_scope_loop = {
							array = ROOT.allies
							
							for_each_scope_loop = {
								array = neighbors
								
								if = {
									limit = {
										NOT = {
											is_in_array = { PREV.PREV.possible_route = THIS }
											is_in_array = { ROOT.allies = THIS }
										}
									}
									
									add_to_array = { PREV.PREV.possible_route = THIS }
								}
							}
						}
						
						for_each_scope_loop = {
							array = possible_route
							
							if = {
								limit = {
									OR = {
										PREV = {
											OR = {
												has_war_with = PREV
												has_wargoal_against = PREV
												is_justifying_wargoal_against = PREV
												
												any_of_scopes = {
													array = faction_members
													
													OR = {
														has_war_with = PREV.PREV
														has_wargoal_against = PREV.PREV
														is_justifying_wargoal_against = PREV.PREV
													}
												}
											}
										}
										
										has_wargoal_against = PREV
										is_justifying_wargoal_against = PREV
										
										any_of_scopes = {
											array = allies
											
											OR = {
												has_war_with = PREV.PREV
												has_wargoal_against = PREV.PREV
												is_justifying_wargoal_against = PREV.PREV
												
												PREV.PREV = {
													OR = {
														has_wargoal_against = PREV
														is_justifying_wargoal_against = PREV
														
														any_of_scopes = {
															array = faction_members
															
															OR = {
																has_war_with = PREV.PREV
																has_wargoal_against = PREV.PREV
																is_justifying_wargoal_against = PREV.PREV
															}
														}
													}
												}
											}
										}
									}
								}
								
								if = {
									limit = {
										OR = {
											is_in_array = { ROOT.neighbors = THIS }
											
											any_of_scopes = {
												array = allies
												
												is_in_array = { ROOT.neighbors = THIS }
											}
											
											any_of_scopes = {
												array = ROOT.allies
												
												OR = {
													is_in_array = { PREV.neighbors = THIS }
													
													any_of_scopes = {
														array = PREV.allies
														
														is_in_array = { PREV.neighbors = THIS }
													}
												}
											}
										}
									}
									
									set_variable = { ROOT.NTR_army_AI_factor = 3 } # possible land war
									set_temp_variable = { break = 1 } # break the loop
								}
								else = {
									for_each_scope_loop = {
										array = neighbors
										
										if = {
											limit = {
												NOT = { is_in_array = { PREV.PREV.possible_route = THIS } }
											}
											
											add_to_array = { PREV.PREV.possible_route = THIS }
										}
									}
								}
							}
							else = {
								remove_from_array = { PREV.possible_route = THIS }
							}
						}
						
						clear_array = possible_route
						
						if = {
							limit = {
								ROOT = { check_variable = { NTR_army_AI_factor = 3 } }
							}
							
							set_temp_variable = { break = 1 } # break the loop
						}
						else = {
							set_variable = { ROOT.NTR_army_AI_factor = 2 } # prepare for land war
						}
					}
				}
			}
			
			################
			 # Threatened #
			################
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { NTR_army_AI_factor < 3 } # bypass
					
					any_other_country = {
						OR = {
							is_justifying_wargoal_against = ROOT
							
							AND = {
								has_wargoal_against = ROOT
								
								NOT = { # essential? #???
									OR = {
										has_non_aggression_pact_with = ROOT
										is_in_faction_with = ROOT
									}
								}
								
								exists = yes

									}

								exists = yes
							}
						}

											is_justifying_wargoal_against = PREV
											
											any_of_scopes = {
												array = allies
												
												OR = {
													has_war_with = PREV.PREV
													has_wargoal_against = PREV.PREV
													is_justifying_wargoal_against = PREV.PREV
													
													PREV.PREV = {
														OR = {
															has_wargoal_against = PREV
															is_justifying_wargoal_against = PREV
															
															any_of_scopes = {
																array = faction_members
																
																OR = {
																	has_war_with = PREV.PREV
																	has_wargoal_against = PREV.PREV
																	is_justifying_wargoal_against = PREV.PREV
																}
															}
														}
													}
												}
											}
										}
									}
									
									if = {
										limit = {
											OR = {
												is_in_array = { PREV.neighbors = THIS }
												
												any_of_scopes = {
													array = allies
													
													is_in_array = { PREV.PREV.neighbors = THIS }
												}
												
												any_of_scopes = {
													array = PREV.allies
													
													OR = {
														is_in_array = { PREV.neighbors = THIS }
														
														any_of_scopes = {
															array = PREV.allies
															
															is_in_array = { PREV.neighbors = THIS }
														}
													}
												}
											}
										}
										
										set_variable = { ROOT.NTR_army_AI_factor = 3 } # possible land war
										set_temp_variable = { break = 1 } # break the loop
									}
									else = {
										for_each_scope_loop = {
											array = neighbors
											
											if = {
												limit = {
													NOT = { is_in_array = { PREV.PREV.possible_route = THIS } }
												}
												
												add_to_array = { PREV.PREV.possible_route = THIS }
											}
										}
									}
								}
								else = {
									remove_from_array = { PREV.possible_route = THIS }
								}
							}
							
							clear_array = possible_route
							
							if = {

									ROOT = { check_variable = { NTR_army_AI_factor = 3 } }
								}

							}
							
							set_variable = { NTR_army_AI_factor = 2 } # prepare for land war
						}
					}

						clear_array = potential_enemies
					}
					
					clear_array = potential_enemies
					clear_array = friends_in_misfortune
				}
			}
			
			##########################
			 # Subjects with Claims #
			##########################
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { NTR_army_AI_factor < 3 } # bypass
				}

						limit = {
							OR = {
								is_justifying_wargoal_against = PREV
								has_wargoal_against = PREV
							}

							limit = {
								NOT = { is_in_array = { ROOT.potential_enemies = THIS } }
							}

						}
					}

									is_in_array = { ROOT.neighbors = THIS }
								}

											is_in_array = { PREV.neighbors = THIS }

									}

				}

			 # Faction Members #
			#####################

					num_faction_members > 1
				}

				 # Members at War #
				####################

					limit = {

							array = faction_members

							NOT = { tag = ROOT }
						}
					}
					
					if = { # neighborhood check
						limit = {
							any_of_scopes = {
								array = faction_members

										is_in_array = { PREV.neighbors = THIS }

											is_in_array = { PREV.PREV.neighbors = THIS }
										}
										
										any_of_scopes = {

							limit = {
								NOT = { tag = ROOT }
							}
							
							every_other_country = {
								limit = {
									OR = {
										is_justifying_wargoal_against = PREV
										
										AND = {
											has_wargoal_against = PREV
											
											NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
										}

							any_other_country = {
								is_guaranteed_by = PREV
								
								any_other_country = {

										is_justifying_wargoal_against = PREV
										
										AND = {
											has_wargoal_against = PREV
											
											NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
										}
									}
								}
							}

								NOT = { tag = ROOT }
							}

								every_other_country = {

										OR = {
											is_justifying_wargoal_against = PREV
											
											AND = {
