								if = {
									limit = {
										NOT = { is_in_array = { ROOT.allies = THIS } }
									}
									
									add_to_array = { PREV.possible_route = THIS }
								}
							}
							
							for_each_scope_loop = {
								array = ROOT.allies
								
								for_each_scope_loop = {
									array = neighbors
									
									if = {
										limit = {
											NOT = {
												is_in_array = { PREV.PREV.possible_route = THIS }
												is_in_array = { ROOT.allies = THIS }
											}
										}
										
										add_to_array = { PREV.PREV.possible_route = THIS }
									}
								}
							}
							
							for_each_scope_loop = {
								array = possible_route
								
								if = {
									limit = {
										OR = {
											PREV = {
												OR = {
													has_war_with = PREV
													has_wargoal_against = PREV
													is_justifying_wargoal_against = PREV
													
													any_of_scopes = {
														array = faction_members
														
														OR = {
															has_war_with = PREV.PREV
															has_wargoal_against = PREV.PREV
															is_justifying_wargoal_against = PREV.PREV
														}
													}
												}
											}
											
											has_wargoal_against = PREV
											is_justifying_wargoal_against = PREV
											
											any_of_scopes = {
												array = allies
												
												OR = {
													has_war_with = PREV.PREV
													has_wargoal_against = PREV.PREV
													is_justifying_wargoal_against = PREV.PREV
													
													PREV.PREV = {
														OR = {
															has_wargoal_against = PREV
															is_justifying_wargoal_against = PREV
															
															any_of_scopes = {
																array = faction_members
																
																OR = {
																	has_war_with = PREV.PREV
																	has_wargoal_against = PREV.PREV
																	is_justifying_wargoal_against = PREV.PREV
																}
															}
														}
													}
												}
											}
										}
									}
									
									if = {
										limit = {
											OR = {
												is_in_array = { ROOT.neighbors = THIS }
												
												any_of_scopes = {
													array = allies
													
													is_in_array = { ROOT.neighbors = THIS }
												}
												
												any_of_scopes = {
													array = ROOT.allies
													
													OR = {
														is_in_array = { PREV.neighbors = THIS }
														
														any_of_scopes = {
															array = PREV.allies
															
															is_in_array = { PREV.neighbors = THIS }
														}
													}
												}
											}
										}
										
										set_variable = { ROOT.NTR_army_AI_factor = 3 } # possible land war
										set_temp_variable = { break = 1 } # break the loop
									}
									else = {
										for_each_scope_loop = {
											array = neighbors
											
											if = {
												limit = {
													NOT = { is_in_array = { PREV.PREV.possible_route = THIS } }
												}
												
												add_to_array = { PREV.PREV.possible_route = THIS }
											}
										}
									}
								}
								else = {
									remove_from_array = { PREV.possible_route = THIS }
								}
							}
							
							clear_array = possible_route
							
							if = {
								limit = {
									ROOT = { check_variable = { NTR_army_AI_factor = 3 } }
								}
								
								set_temp_variable = { break = 1 } # break the loop
							}
						}
						
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { NTR_army_AI_factor < 2 }
							}
							
							set_variable = { NTR_army_AI_factor = 2 } # prepare for land war
						}
					}
					
					clear_array = potential_enemies
				}
			}
		}
		
		if = { # pre-check for naval AI behavior
			limit = {
				any_of_scopes = {
					array = controlled_states
					
					is_coastal = yes
				}
			}
			
			if = { # check for possible naval war
				limit = {
					any_of_scopes = {
						array = potential_enemies
						
						OR = {
							any_of_scopes = {
								array = controlled_states
								
								is_coastal = yes
							}
							
							any_of_scopes = {
								array = allies
								
								any_of_scopes = {
									array = controlled_states
									
									is_coastal = yes
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { NTR_army_AI_factor = 2 } # no possible connections (for now)
					}
					
					set_variable = { NTR_navy_AI_factor = 5 } # rush navy
				}
				else = { # possible land and naval war
					set_variable = { NTR_navy_AI_factor = 3 } # focus on navy
				}
			}
			else = { # no naval war -> increase land priority (possible aggressive meatball)
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { NTR_army_AI_factor = 3 }
					}
					
					set_variable = { NTR_army_AI_factor = 5 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { NTR_army_AI_factor = 2 }
					}
					
					set_variable = { NTR_army_AI_factor = 3 }
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_variable = { NTR_navy_AI_factor = 1 } # default navy factor
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { NTR_army_AI_factor > NTR_navy_AI_factor }
			}
			
			set_variable = { NTR_threat_AI_factor = NTR_army_AI_factor }
		}
		else = {
			set_variable = { NTR_threat_AI_factor = NTR_navy_AI_factor }
		}
		
		set_variable = { NTR_air_AI_factor = NTR_army_AI_factor }
		add_to_variable = { NTR_air_AI_factor = NTR_navy_AI_factor }
		divide_variable = { NTR_air_AI_factor = 2 } # 2-6 -> 1-3
		
		# Checks for production behavior
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { num_target_equipment_in_armies_k@infantry_equipment > num_equipment_in_armies_k@infantry_equipment }
			}
			
			set_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = num_target_equipment_in_armies_k@infantry_equipment }
			divide_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = num_equipment_in_armies_k@infantry_equipment }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = 1 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = NTR_army_AI_factor }
			add_to_variable = { NTR_war_production_AI_factor = AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { num_target_equipment_in_armies_k@magical_equipment > num_equipment_in_armies_k@magical_equipment }
			}
			
			set_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = num_target_equipment_in_armies_k@magical_equipment }
			divide_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = num_equipment_in_armies_k@magical_equipment }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = 1 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = NTR_army_AI_factor }
			add_to_variable = { NTR_war_production_AI_factor = AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { num_target_equipment_in_armies_k@support_equipment > num_equipment_in_armies_k@support_equipment }
			}
			
			set_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = num_target_equipment_in_armies_k@support_equipment }
			divide_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = num_equipment_in_armies_k@support_equipment }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = 1 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = NTR_army_AI_factor }
			add_to_variable = { NTR_war_production_AI_factor = AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { num_target_equipment_in_armies_k@support_equipment > num_equipment_in_armies_k@support_equipment }
			}
			
			set_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = num_target_equipment_in_armies_k@support_equipment }
			divide_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = num_equipment_in_armies_k@support_equipment }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = 1 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = NTR_army_AI_factor }
			add_to_variable = { NTR_war_production_AI_factor = AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { num_target_equipment_in_armies_k@artillery_equipment > num_equipment_in_armies_k@artillery_equipment }
			}
			
			set_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = num_target_equipment_in_armies_k@artillery_equipment }
			divide_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = num_equipment_in_armies_k@artillery_equipment }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = 1 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = NTR_army_AI_factor }
			add_to_variable = { NTR_war_production_AI_factor = AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { num_target_equipment_in_armies_k@anti_air_equipment > num_equipment_in_armies_k@anti_air_equipment }
			}
			
			set_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = num_target_equipment_in_armies_k@anti_air_equipment }
			divide_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = num_equipment_in_armies_k@anti_air_equipment }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = 1 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = NTR_army_AI_factor }
			add_to_variable = { NTR_war_production_AI_factor = AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { num_target_equipment_in_armies_k@anti_tank_equipment > num_equipment_in_armies_k@anti_tank_equipment }
			}
			
			set_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = num_target_equipment_in_armies_k@anti_tank_equipment }
			divide_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = num_equipment_in_armies_k@anti_tank_equipment }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = 1 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = NTR_army_AI_factor }
			add_to_variable = { NTR_war_production_AI_factor = AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { num_target_equipment_in_armies_k@mechanized_equipment > num_equipment_in_armies_k@mechanized_equipment }
			}
			
			set_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = num_target_equipment_in_armies_k@mechanized_equipment }
			divide_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = num_equipment_in_armies_k@mechanized_equipment }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = 1 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = NTR_army_AI_factor }
			add_to_variable = { NTR_war_production_AI_factor = AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { num_target_equipment_in_armies_k@amphibious_mechanized_equipment > num_equipment_in_armies_k@amphibious_mechanized_equipment }
			}
			
			set_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = num_target_equipment_in_armies_k@amphibious_mechanized_equipment }
			divide_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = num_equipment_in_armies_k@amphibious_mechanized_equipment }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = 1 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = NTR_army_AI_factor }
			add_to_variable = { NTR_war_production_AI_factor = AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { num_target_equipment_in_armies_k@light_tank_equipment > num_equipment_in_armies_k@light_tank_equipment }
			}
			
			set_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = num_target_equipment_in_armies_k@light_tank_equipment }
			divide_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = num_equipment_in_armies_k@light_tank_equipment }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = 1 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = NTR_army_AI_factor }
			add_to_variable = { NTR_war_production_AI_factor = AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { num_target_equipment_in_armies_k@medium_tank_equipment > num_equipment_in_armies_k@medium_tank_equipment }
			}
			
			set_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = num_target_equipment_in_armies_k@medium_tank_equipment }
			divide_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = num_equipment_in_armies_k@medium_tank_equipment }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = 1 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = NTR_army_AI_factor }
			add_to_variable = { NTR_war_production_AI_factor = AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { num_target_equipment_in_armies_k@heavy_tank_equipment > num_equipment_in_armies_k@heavy_tank_equipment }
			}
			
			set_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = num_target_equipment_in_armies_k@heavy_tank_equipment }
			divide_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = num_equipment_in_armies_k@heavy_tank_equipment }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = 1 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = NTR_army_AI_factor }
			add_to_variable = { NTR_war_production_AI_factor = AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { num_target_equipment_in_armies_k@super_heavy_tank_equipment > num_equipment_in_armies_k@super_heavy_tank_equipment }
			}
			
			set_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = num_target_equipment_in_armies_k@super_heavy_tank_equipment }
			divide_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = num_equipment_in_armies_k@super_heavy_tank_equipment }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = 1 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = NTR_army_AI_factor }
			add_to_variable = { NTR_war_production_AI_factor = AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { num_target_equipment_in_armies_k@modern_tank_equipment > num_equipment_in_armies_k@modern_tank_equipment }
			}
			
			set_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = num_target_equipment_in_armies_k@modern_tank_equipment }
			divide_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = num_equipment_in_armies_k@modern_tank_equipment }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = 1 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = NTR_army_AI_factor }
			add_to_variable = { NTR_war_production_AI_factor = AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { num_target_equipment_in_armies_k@amphibious_tank_equipment > num_equipment_in_armies_k@amphibious_tank_equipment }
			}
			
			set_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = num_target_equipment_in_armies_k@amphibious_tank_equipment }
			divide_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = num_equipment_in_armies_k@amphibious_tank_equipment }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = 1 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var = NTR_army_AI_factor }
			add_to_variable = { NTR_war_production_AI_factor = AI_production_equipment_ratio_temp_var }
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				amount_research_slots > 0
			}
			
			# The better your research base, the less impact bonuses add to your research
			
			set_temp_variable = { NTR_research_priority_temp_var = 1 }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { NTR_research_priority_temp_var = modifier@research_speed_factor }
			divide_temp_variable = { NTR_research_priority_temp_var = amount_research_slots }
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { NTR_war_production_AI_factor > 1 }
				}
				
				set_variable = { NTR_army_research_AI_factor = 0 } # focus on production (don't change lines)
			}
			else = {
				set_variable = { NTR_army_research_AI_factor = NTR_army_AI_factor }
				multiply_variable = { NTR_army_research_AI_factor = NTR_research_priority_temp_var }
				multiply_variable = { NTR_army_research_AI_factor = NTR_war_production_AI_factor }
			}
			
			set_variable = { NTR_navy_research_AI_factor = NTR_navy_AI_factor }
			multiply_variable = { NTR_navy_research_AI_factor = NTR_research_priority_temp_var }
			set_variable = { NTR_air_research_AI_factor = NTR_air_AI_factor }
			multiply_variable = { NTR_air_research_AI_factor = NTR_research_priority_temp_var }
		}
		else = {
			set_variable = { NTR_army_research_AI_factor = 0 }
			set_variable = { NTR_navy_research_AI_factor = 0 }
			set_variable = { NTR_air_research_AI_factor = 0 }
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				num_of_military_factories > 0
			}
			
			if = { # "Construct or Modernize"
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						check_variable = { resource@rubber < 0 }
						check_variable = { resource@aluminium < 0 }
						check_variable = { resource@tungsten < 0 }
						check_variable = { resource@chromium < 0 }
						check_variable = { resource@crystals < 0 }
						check_variable = { resource@steel < 0 }
					}
				}
				
				set_variable = { NTR_war_construction_AI_factor = 0.5 }
				add_to_variable = { NTR_war_construction_AI_factor = modifier@production_factory_max_efficiency_factor }
				multiply_variable = { NTR_war_construction_AI_factor = modifier@industrial_capacity_factory }
				divide_variable = { NTR_war_construction_AI_factor = num_of_military_factories }
				
				clamp_variable = {
					var = NTR_war_construction_AI_factor
					max = 1
				}
				
				multiply_variable = { NTR_war_construction_AI_factor = NTR_war_production_AI_factor }
				subtract_from_variable = { NTR_war_production_AI_factor = NTR_war_construction_AI_factor }
			}
			else = {
				set_variable = { NTR_war_construction_AI_factor = 0 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_variable = { NTR_war_construction_AI_factor = NTR_war_production_AI_factor }
			set_variable = { NTR_war_production_AI_factor = 0 }
		}
	}
}
